本文件代替 GB 18030 一 2005 信息技术 ”中文编码字符集与 GB 18030 一 2005 相比,除结构调整和编辑性改动外,主要扩术变化如下:	This document replaces GB 18030-2005 Information Technology "Chinese coded character set compared with GB 18030-2005, except for structural adjustments and editorial changes, the main expansion changes are as follows:	yes

在双字节编码区更改了 10 个竖排标点和8 个汉字构件所对应的 GB/I 13000 代码位置,并其除了 6 个重复编码的汉字构件和 9 个重复编码的汉字( 见附录 D,2005 年版的附录A)，	The GB/I 13000 code position corresponding to 10 vertical punctuation points and 8 Chinese character components has been changed in the double-byte coding area, and in addition to 6 repeatedly encoded Chinese character components and 9 repeatedly encoded Chinese characters (see Appendix D, Appendix A of the 2005 edition)，	yes
在四字节编码区更改了18 个 GB/T 13000 代码位置(见附录 D,2005 年版的附录D);	18 GB/T 13000 code positions have been changed in the four-byte encoding area (see Appendix D, Appendix D of the 2005 edition);	yes
删除了附录 ”追加的汉字及部首/部件 “ 见 2005 年版的附录 〇 ，	The appendix ”Additional Chinese characters and radicals/parts" has been deleted. See Appendix 〇 of the 2005 edition. ，	yes
增加了实现的级别 " (见第9草);	Increased the level of realization" (see chapter 9);	yes

信息扩术 ”中文编码字符集	Information Expansion "Chinese Coded Character Set	yes
1 本文件规定了信息技术用的中文图形字符及甚二进制编码的十六进制表示 。	1This document specifies the hexadecimal representation of Chinese graphic characters and even binary encoding used in information technology.	yes
本文件适用于中文和其他文字图形字符信息的处理、交换、存储、传给、显现 、输入和输出。	This document is suitable for the processing, exchange, storage, transmission, display, input and output of Chinese and other text, graphic and character information.	no
本文件适用于为具备中文和其他文字图形字符信息化处理及交换功能的技术类产品,包括但不限于以输入法、光学字符识别 (OCR)、编辑 校对、机融翻诺、语音合成、文字转写、乔能写作等为代表的软件产品 , 以及以计算机、通信终端设备、电子书阅读毅、学习机等为代表的便件产品 。	This document is suitable for technical products with information processing and exchange functions of Chinese and other text, graphics and characters, including but not limited to input methods, optical character recognition (OCR), editing and proofreading, machine fusion translation, speech synthesis, text transcription, Qiao Neng writing, etc. Software products, as well as portable products represented by computers, communication terminal equipment, e-book readers, learning machines, etc.	no

其中, 注日期的引用文件,仅该日期对应的版本适用于本文件;不注日期的引用文件,其最新厂本(包括所有的修改单)适用于本文件。	Among them, for dated reference documents, only the version corresponding to that date is applicable to this document; for undated reference documents, the latest factory version (including all modification orders) is applicable to this document.	no

GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030 A 2022	no
4 字汇	4 vocabulary	no
4.1 概述	4.1 Overview	no
本文件收录的字符以单字节、双字或四字节编码 。	The characters included in this document are encoded in single-byte, double-character, or four-byte.	no
单字节部分收录了 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的 0x00~0x7F 全部 128 个字符 。	The single-byte part contains all 128 characters from 0x00~0x7F of GB/T 11383-1989.	no
4.3 双字节部分	4.3 Double-byte part	no
双字节部分收录了 GB/T 2312 一 1980 中的全部图形字符 GB/T 13000 中的CJK 统一汉字以及部分图形字符。	The double-byte part contains all the graphic characters in GB/T 2312-1980, the CJK unified Chinese characters in GB/T 13000, and some graphic characters.	no
双字节部分的字符按照附录 A 的规定。	The characters of the double-byte part are in accordance with the provisions of Appendix A.	no
其中,表意文字描述符的图形、代码位置和功能应符合附录 B 的规定 。	Among them, the graphics, code location and functions of the ideographic character descriptors should comply with the provisions of Appendix B.	no
注: GB/T 13000 对中国、日本、恩国、越南等国家和地区使用的汉字统一编码。	Note: GB/T 13000 uniformly encodes Chinese characters used in China, Japan, Enguo, Vietnam and other countries and regions.	no
具备独有抽象字形的汉字,赋予单独的代码位置;来源不同而抽象字形相同的汉字, 则赋予共用的代码位置。	Chinese characters with unique abstract glyphs are given a separate code position; Chinese characters with different sources and the same abstract glyphs are given a common code position.	no
经过编码的汉字称为CJK 统一汉字 CCJK Unified Ideographs,其中 CJK 表示中国、日本、韩国。	The encoded Chinese characters are called CJK Unified Chinese characters CCJK Unified Ideographs, where CJK represents China, Japan, and South Korea.	no
4.4 四字节部分	4.4 Four-byte part	no
四字节部分收录了上述双字节字符之外的 GB/T 13000 中的 66 个CJK统一汉字(9FA6 一 9FEF，不包括 9FB4~9FBB 的8个字符)、CJK 统一汉字扩充 A、CJK 统一汉字扩充 BCJK 统一汉字扩充 C、 CJK 统一汉字扩充 DCJK 统一汉字扩充下 .CJK 统一汉字扩充 F 和已经 在 GB/ 工 13000 中编码的少数民族文字的字符。	The four-byte part contains 66 CJK unified Chinese characters in GB/T 13000 other than the above two-byte characters (9FA6 to 9FEF, excluding 8 characters from 9FB4 to 9FBB), CJK unified Chinese character expansion A, CJK unified Chinese character expansion BCJK Unified Chinese character expansion C, CJK Unified Chinese character expansion DCJK Unified Chinese character Expansion.CJK unified Chinese character expansion F and the characters of ethnic minority characters that have been encoded in GB/T 13000.	no
四字节部分的字符按照附录 C 的规定 。	The characters in the four-byte part are in accordance with the provisions of Appendix C.	no
5 总体结构	5 Overall structure	no
正文中凡数字前标有 0x 的表示采用十六进制,未标有 0x 的表示采用十进制。	In the text, all numbers marked with 0x before them are in hexadecimal, and those not marked with 0x are in decimal.	no
附录中凡编码的表示均采用十六进制,其他数字的表示均采用十进制。	The representation of all encodings in the appendix is in hexadecimal, and the representation of other numbers is in decimal.	no
单字节部分采用 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的编码结构,使 用 0x00~0x7F 码位。	The single-byte part adopts the coding structure of GB/T 11383-1989, using 0x00~0x7F code points.	no
双字贡部分采用两个八位二进制位串表示一个字符,其首字节码位从 0x81 一 0xFE, 尾字节码位分别是 0x40 一 0x7E 和 0x80 一 0xFE。	The double-character character part uses two eight-bit binary bit strings to represent a character, the first byte code point is from 0x81 to 0xFE, and the last byte code point is 0x40 to 0x7E and 0x80 to 0xFE, respectively.	no
四字节部分采用 GB/工 11383 一 1989 未采用的 0x30 一 0x39 作为对双字节编码扩充的后缀,编码范围为 0x81308130 一 0xFE39FE39。	The four-byte part adopts the 0x30-0x39 not used in GB/T 11383-1989 as the suffix for the expansion of the two-byte encoding, and the encoding range is 0x81308130-0xFE39FE39.	no
四字节字符的第一个字厄编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第二个字记编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39; 第三个字节编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第 四个字市编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39。 即 : 0x81308130 一 0x81308139; 0x81308230 一 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 一 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 一 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c “0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 一 0xFE39FE39 。	The encoding range of the first character of a four-byte character is 0x81 to 0xFE; the encoding range of the second character is 0x30 to 0x39; the encoding range of the third byte is 0x81 to 0xFE; the encoding range of the fourth character is 0x30 to 0x39. Namely: 0x81308130 a 0x81308139; 0x81308230 a 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 a 0x8130fe39; 0x81318130 A 0x81318139; Oo2douolag0c “0uro23061393 0xFE39FE30 A 0xFE39FE39.	no
总体结构与码位范围分配见图 1 和表 1。	The overall structure and code point range allocation are shown in Figure 1 and Table 1.	no
6 字符的排列顺序	Order of 6 characters	no
6.1 单字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.1 The order of some characters in a single word brush	no
单字记部分字符按照 GB/I 11383 一 1989 中相应字符的顺序排列 。	The characters of the single-character notation are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in GB/I 11383-1989.	no
6.2 双字市部分字符的排列顺序	6.2 The order of some characters in the double-character city	no
双字下部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 A。	The order of the characters in the lower part of the double characters should conform to Appendix A.	no
6.3 四字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.3 The order of some characters in the four-character brush	no
自 0x81308130 至 0x8439FE39 共 50400 个码位,对应双字节部分未包括的所有 GB/T 13000 基本多文种平面的字符,按照GB/T13000 基本多文种平面相应字符的顺序排列 。	There are a total of 50,400 code points from 0x81308130 to 0x8439FE39, corresponding to all the characters of the GB/T 13000 basic multilingual plane not included in the double-byte part, arranged in the order of the corresponding characters of the GB/T 13000 basic multilingual plane.	no
自 0x90308130 至 0xE339FE39 共 1058400 个码位用于对应 GB/T 13000 的16个辅助平面,字符排列顺序完全按照 GB/I 13000 的 16个辅助平面的相应码位顺序依次排列 。	From 0x90308130 to 0xE339FE39, a total of 1058,400 code points are used to correspond to the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/T 13000. The order of characters is exactly in accordance with the corresponding code points of the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/I 13000.	no
四字节部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 C。	The order of the characters in the four-byte part should conform to Appendix C.	no

9.1 通则	9.1 General Rules	yes
本文件规定三个实现级别。	This document specifies three implementation levels.	yes
符合相应实现级别的系统软件产品,应提供相应实现级别范围内全部字符的输入输出功能。	System software products that meet the corresponding implementation level shall provide input and output functions for all characters within the scope of the corresponding implementation level.	yes
9.2 实现级别 1	9.2 Implementation level 1	yes
实现级别 1 文持本文件的单字节编码部分、双季节编码部分和四字下编玛部分的 CJK 统一汉字 ( 即 0x82358F33 一 0x82359636) 和 CJK 统一汉字扩A( 即 0x8139EE39 一 0x82358738) 。	Implement level 1 text to support the CJK unified Chinese characters (i.e. 0x82358F33-0x82359636) and CJK unified Chinese character expansion A (i.e. 0x8139EE39-0x82358738) of the single-byte encoded part, the two-byte encoded part, and the four-character encoded part of this document.	yes
任何本文件适用的产品均应满足实现级别 1 的要求。	Any product applicable to this document shall meet the requirements of implementation level 1.	yes
注: 根据软件应用需要 ,实现级别 1 还可选择文持表 3 列出的任何一种或多种非汉字文种。	Note: According to the needs of software applications, implementation level 1 can also choose any one or more non-Chinese characters listed in Table 3.	no
9.3 实现级别 2	9.3 Implementation level 2	no
实现级别 2 包含实现级别 1。	Implementation level 2 includes implementation level 1.	no
此外 ,实现级别 2 还文持《通用 规范 汉字 表 }中的没有包合在实级别 1 之内的编码汉字。	In addition, implementation level 2 also supports coded Chinese characters that are not included in the "General Specification Chinese Character Table" that are not included in real level 1.	no
《 通用规范汉字表) 所收汉字在本文件中的代码位置和字形, 见附录下。	The code position and glyphs of the received Chinese characters in this document in the "General Specification Chinese Character Table" are shown in the appendix.	no
系统软件及支撑软件,应满足实现级别 2 的要求 。	The system software and support software should meet the requirements of implementation level 2.	no
注: 系统软件及文撑软件包括但不限于操作系统,数据库管理系统.中间件( 软件产品分类的信息见 GB/ 工 36475)。	Note: System software and document support software include but are not limited to operating system, database management system.Middleware (see GB/T 36475 for information on software product classification).	no
9.4 实现级别 3	9.4 Implementation level 3	no
实现级别 3 包含实现级别 2。	Implementation level 3 includes implementation level 2.	no
此外,实现级别 3 还文持本文件规定的全部汉字及表 3 中的康黑部首。	In addition, realization level 3 also supports all Chinese characters specified in this document and the Kanghe radicals in Table 3.	no
用于政务服务和公共服务的产品应满足实现级卉 3 的要求。	Products used in government services and public services should meet the requirements of implementation level 3.	no
注: 政务服务和 共服务行业包括但不限于铁路运输业.道路运输业 \ 水上运输业.航空运输业、多式联运和运输代理业、邮政业、货币金融服、保险业、土地、管理业、卫生、国家机构、社会保障等 (行业分类的信息见 GB/ 工 4754)。	Note: Government services and public service industries include but are not limited to the railway transportation industry.Road transport industry \ water transport industry.Air transport industry, multimodal transport and transportation agency industry, postal industry, currency and financial services, insurance industry, land, management industry, health, state institutions, social security, etc. (See GB/T 4754 for industry classification information).	no

描述 (DESCRIPTION) C 和 C++ 编译器是集成的.他们都要用四个步骤中的一个或多个处理输入文件: 预处理(preprocessing), Hii(compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking) .	DESCRIPTION THE C AND C++ COMPILERS ARE INTEGRATED.They all use one or more of the four steps to process the input file: preprocessing (preprocessing), Hii (compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking).	yes
源文件后级名标识源文件的语言, 但是对编译器来说, 后绥名控制着缺省设定:	The post-level name of the source file identifies the language of the source file, but for the compiler, the post-level name controls the default setting:	yes

了的目标文件.	The target file.	yes
编译后即停止, 不进行汇编件.	It will stop after compilation and will not be assembled.	yes
在编译过程的不同阶段间使用管道而非临时文件进行工作, 因为那些系统的汇编器不能从管道读取数据，GNU 的汇编器没有这个问题，汇编器能够接受的 C "方言 ": 支持符合 ANSI 标准的 C 程序.	Use pipelines instead of temporary files to work at different stages of the compilation process, because the assemblers of those systems cannot read data from pipelines. The assembler of GNU does not have this problem. The C "dialect" that the assembler can accept: Supports C programs that comply with ANSI standards.	yes
这样就会关闭 GNU Cc 中某些不兼容 ANSI Cc 的特性关键字, 以及诸如 unix 和 vax 这些表明当迎和极少使用的 ANSI trigraph 特性,以及禁上尽管使 用了(译注 :宿主环境 (hosted environment) 下所有的标准库可用，main 函数返回 一个 int 值, 典型例子是除了内核以外几乎所有的程序.对应的独立环境 (f£reestanding environment) 不存在标准库, 程序入口也不一定是 main, 最明显的例子就是操作系统内核.详情参考 gcc 网站最近的资料)	This will turn off some feature keywords in GNU Cc that are not compatible with ANSI Cc, as well as ANSI trigraph features such as unix and vax that indicate that they are popular and rarely used, and prohibit the use of (Translation note: All standard libraries under the hosted environment are available, and the main function returns an int value, a typical example is almost all programs except the kernel.The corresponding independent environment (f£reestanding environment) does not have a standard library, and the program entry is not necessarily main. The most obvious example is the operating system kernel.Refer to the recent information on the gcc website for details)	yes
对于没有参数的函数声明, 例如 `int foo ();', 按 C 风格处理 --- 即不说明参数个数或类型. (仅针对 C++) .	For function declarations without parameters, such as'int foo ();', they are processed in C style -that is, the number or type of parameters are not stated. (For C++ only).	no
正常情况下, 这样的函数 foo 在 C++ 中意味着参数为空.	Under normal circumstances, such a function foo in C++ means that the parameter is empty.	no
节清单从这里删到试图支持传统 C 编译器的某些方面.	The section list is deleted from here to try to support some aspects of traditional C compilers.	no
详见NU c 手册,我们已经把细节删除, 这样当内容过时后, 人们也不会 HERI.	See the NU c manual for details. We have deleted the details so that when the content is outdated, people will not HERI.	no
除了一件事: 对于 c++ 程序 (不是C)，` -traditional' 选项带来一个附加效应,允许对 this 赋值.	Except for one thing: for c++ programs (not C), the`-traditional' option has an additional effect, allowing this to be assigned a value.	no
他和`-Ethis-is-variable' 选项的果一样.	He has the same effect as the`-Ethis-is-variable' option.	no
-traditional-cpp 试图支持传统 Cc 预处理器的某些方面.	-traditional-cpp tries to support certain aspects of traditional Cc preprocessors.	no
特别是上面提到有关预处理器的内容, 但是不包括 `-traditional' 选项的其他效应.	In particular, the content about preprocessors mentioned above, but does not include other effects of the`-traditional' option.	no
-fdollars-in-identifiers 允许在标识符 (identifier) 中使用 `$' 字符 (仅针对 C++) .	-fdollars-in-identifiers allows the use of the `$' character in the identifier (for C++ only).	no
你可以指定 `“-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' 选项显明禁止使用 `$' 符.	You can specify the'"-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers` option to explicitly prohibit the use of the'$' character.	no
(GNU C++ 在某些目标系统缺省允许 `$' 符, 但不是所有系统.)	(GNU C++ allows the`$' character by default on some target systems, but not all systems.)	no
-fenum-int-equiv 允许 ant 类型到枚举类型 (enumeration) 的隐式转换 (MEF c++) .	-fenum-int-equiv allows the implicit conversion of ant type to enumeration type (MEF c++).	no
正常情况下 GNU C++ 允许从 enum 到 int 的转换,反之则不行.	Under normal circumstances, GNU C++ allows conversion from enum to int, but vice versa.	no
-fexternal-—templates 为模板声明 (template declaration) 产生较小的代码 (仅限于 c++)，方法是对于每个模板函数 (template function),只在 定义他们的地方生成一个副本.	-fexonal--templates generates smaller code (limited to c++) for template declaration by generating only one copy of each template function where they are defined for each template function.	no
想要成功使用这个选项, 你必须在所有使用模板的文件中,标记`#pragma implementatio'(定义)或 `#Pragma interface'(声明).	To successfully use this option, you must mark`#Pragma implements' (definition) or`#Pragma interface' (declaration) in all files that use the template.	no
程序用 `-fexternal-templates ' 编译时, 模板实例 (template instantiation) 全部是外部类型.你必须让需要的实例在实现文件中出现.	When the program is compiled with`-fexental-templates', the template instantiation is all external types.You must make the required instance appear in the implementation file.	no
可以通过 typedef 实现这一点, 他引用所需的每个实例.	This can be achieved through typedef, which refers to each instance required.	no
相对应的, 如果编译时使用缺省选项 ` -fno-exteznal-templates', 所有模板实例明确的设为内置.	Correspondingly, if the default option`-fno-exteznal-templates' is used at compile time, all template instances are explicitly set to built-in.	no
所有的成员函数(除了构造子函数和 mnew 或 delete 成员操作符) 视为所在类的虚函数.	All member functions (except constructor functions and mnew or delete member operators) are regarded as virtual functions of the class in which they are located.	no
这不表明每次调用成员函数都将通过内部虚函数表.	This does not mean that every time a member function is called, it will pass through the internal virtual function table.	no
有些情况下, 编译器能够判断出可以直接调用某个虚函数; 这时就直接调用.	In some cases, the compiler can judge that a virtual function can be called directly; at this time, it is called directly.	no
-fcond-mismatch 允许条件表达式的第二和第三个参数的类型不匹配.	-fcond-mismatch allows the types of the second and third parameters of the conditional expression to not match.	no
这种表达式的值是 Void.-fthis-—is-variable 允许对 this 赋值 (仅对 c++).	The value of this expression is Void.-fthis--is-variable allows assigning a value to this (only for c++).	no
合并用户自定义的自由存储管理机制到 c++ 后,使可赋值的`this' 显得不合时宜.	After merging the user-defined free storage management mechanism into c++, the assignable'this` seems anachronistic.	no
因此, 默认情况下, 类成员函数内部对 this 赋值是无效操作.	Therefore, by default, assigning a value to this inside a class member function is an invalid operation.	no
然而为了向后兼容, 你可以通过 `-fthis-is-variable' 选项使这种操作有效.	However, for backward compatibility, you can use the'-fthis-is-variable' option to make this operation effective.	no
-funsigned-char 把 char 定义为无符号类型,如同 unsigned char.	-funsigned-char defines char as an unsigned type, just like unsigned char.	no
各种机器都有自己缺省的 char 类型. 既可能是 unsigned char 也可能是 signed char.	Various machines have their own default char type. It may be either unsigned char or signed char.	no
理想情况下, 当依赖于数据的符号性时, 一个可移植程序总是应该使用 signed char 或 unsigned chaz.	Ideally, when relying on the symbolicity of the data, a portable program should always use signed char or unsigned chaz.	no
但是许多程序已经写成只用简单的 char, 并且期街这是有符号数(或者无符号数, 具体情况取决于编写程序的目标机器).	But many programs have been written to use only simple char, and it is expected that this is a signed number (or an unsigned number, depending on the target machine where the program is written).	no
这个选项, 和它的反义选项, 使那样的程序工作在对应的默认值上.	This option, and its antisense option, make such a program work on the corresponding default value.	no
char 的类型始终应该明确定义为 signed char 或 unsigned char, 即使它表现的和其中之一完全一样.	The type of char should always be clearly defined as signed char or unsigned char, even if it behaves exactly the same as one of them.	no
如果没有明确声明 ` signed' 或 "unsigned'修饰符, 这些选项用来定义有符号位域 (bitfield) 或无符号位域.	If the'signed` or'unsigned' modifiers are not explicitly declared, these options are used to define a signed bitfield or an unsigned bitfield.	no
缺省情况下,位域是有符号的, 因为他们继承的基本整数类型,如 int,是有符号数，然而, 如果指定了 `-traditional' 选项,位域永远是无符号数.	By default, bit fields are signed because the basic integer types they inherit, such as int, are signed numbers. However, if the`-traditional' option is specified, the bit fields will always be unsigned numbers.	no
-fwritable-strings把字符串常量存储到可写数据段, 而且不做特别对待.	-fwritable-strings stores string constants in writable data segments without special treatment.	no
这是为了兼容一些老程序,他们算改字符串常量是一个非常糟糕的想法、`-traditional' 选项也有相同效果.	This is to be compatible with some old programs. It is a very bad idea for them to change the string constant. The`-traditional' option has the same effect.	no
执行摘要	Executive Summary	yes
新冠肺炎对毒品市场的影响	The impact of the new crown pneumonia on the drug market	yes
其影响可能类似于2008年的经济危机	The impact may be similar to the 2008 economic crisis	yes
全球性的新冠肺炎疫情已使全世界陷入前所未有的危机。	The global new crown pneumonia epidemic has plunged the world into an unprecedented crisis.	yes
在许多国家，这一疾病己使医疗服务机构穷于应付，几近崩溃，各国政府实施的限制措施已在全球经济中造成了严重紊乱。	In many countries, the disease has made medical services overwhelmed and almost collapsed. The restrictive measures implemented by governments have caused serious disorders in the global economy.	yes
对于毒品市场，这场疫情的影响尚不清楚，也很难预测，但有可能影响深远。	For the drug market, the impact of this epidemic is not yet clear and difficult to predict, but it may have a far-reaching impact.	yes
一些生产者可能会被迫寻找新的方法来制造毒品，因为限制流动的同时也限制了前体和基本化学品的获取。	Some producers may be forced to find new ways to make drugs, because restrictions on movement also restrict access to precursors and basic chemicals.	yes
贩运者由于旅行限制而无法越境，可能不得不寻找新的路线和方法。	Traffickers are unable to cross the border due to travel restrictions and may have to find new routes and methods.	yes
毒品使用和提供的模式可能会改变，政府的应对能力也可能会受到阻碍。	The patterns of drug use and provision may change, and the government's ability to respond may also be hindered.	yes
新冠肺炎带来的转变是前所未有的，但还是可以从以往的危机中吸取一些经验教训。	The changes brought about by the new crown pneumonia are unprecedented, but some lessons can still be learned from previous crises.	yes
2008年经济危机后，一些吸毒者开始寻找更便宜的合成物质，使用模式转向注射毒品。	After the 2008 economic crisis, some drug addicts began to look for cheaper synthetic substances, and their use patterns turned to injecting drugs.	no
与此同时，各国政府削减了与毒品相关的预算。	At the same time, governments have cut drug-related budgets.	no
如果各国政府以同样的方式应对当前的经济衰退，预防吸毒和相关风险行为等干预措施和戒毒治疗服务可能会受到沉重打击。	If governments respond to the current economic recession in the same way, interventions such as drug abuse prevention and related risky behaviors and drug treatment services may be hit hard.	no
此外，拦截行动和国际合作的优先性可能会降低，使贩运者更容易行动。	In addition, the priority of interception operations and international cooperation may be reduced, making it easier for traffickers to move.	no
一些国家有大量毒品通过商业航班走私，预计这些国家的贩毒活动受到的直接影响最大。	A large number of drugs are smuggled through commercial flights in some countries, and it is expected that drug trafficking activities in these countries will be directly affected the most.	no
有信使将甲基苯丙胺等合成毒品放在随身背包或藏在私人行李中携带，有时数量很大。由于几乎各地都对航空客运实施了限制，利用商业航空旅行供应毒品的活动可能会完全中断。	Some couriers carry synthetic drugs such as methamphetamine in carry-on backpacks or hidden in personal luggage, sometimes in large quantities.Due to restrictions on air passenger transportation in almost all places, the use of commercial air travel to supply drugs may be completely interrupted.	no
尽管国际邮政供应链也受到了干扰，但利用暗网和货物邮寄进行贩运的活动可能会增加。	Although the international postal supply chain has also been disrupted, the use of the dark Web and the mailing of goods for trafficking may increase.	no
从长远来看，经济衰退和相关的封闭措施可能会打乱毒品市场。	In the long run, the economic recession and related closure measures may disrupt the drug market.	no
由于不断上升的失业率和缺乏机会，贫困和弱势人群将更有可能以有害的方式吸毒，患上吸毒病症，并转向与毒品有关的非法活动一无论是生产还是运输。	Due to rising unemployment and lack of opportunities, poor and vulnerable people will be more likely to take drugs in harmful ways, suffer from drug abuse disorders, and turn to illegal drug-related activities, whether it is production or transportation.	no
贩毒组织可能会利用这种情况，向脆弱人群提供服务，并招募新成员来壮大队伍。	Drug trafficking organizations may take advantage of this situation to provide services to vulnerable groups and recruit new members to strengthen their teams.	no
随着政府应对能力的降低，这些转变可能会快速扎根，成为许多社区的新现实。	As the government's ability to respond decreases, these changes may quickly take root and become a new reality for many communities.	no
扩张与复杂性	Expansion and complexity	no
市场增长	Market growth	no
人口增长模式部分解释了市场扩张的原因	The population growth model partly explains the reasons for market expansion	no
世界各地的吸毒现象一直在增多，无论是从总体数字还是从吸毒者在世界人口中所占比例来看都是如此。	The phenomenon of drug abuse around the world has been increasing, both in terms of overall figures and the proportion of drug users in the world's population.	no
2009年估计吸毒者有2.1亿人，占全球15-64岁人口的4.8%,而2018年估计吸毒者有2.69亿人，占这类人口的5.3%。	In 2009, it was estimated that there were 210 million drug addicts, accounting for 4.8% of the global population aged 15-64, while in 2018, it was estimated that there were 269 million drug addicts, accounting for 5.3% of this population.	no
在过去二十年期间，发展中国家吸毒情况的增长速度远远快于发达国家。	During the past two decades, the growth rate of drug abuse in developing countries has been much faster than that of developed countries.	no
这在一定程度上反映了这一期间总体人口增长的差异、发达国家为7%,发展中国家为28%但也反映了发展中国家年 轻人口增长较快。	This reflects to a certain extent the difference in overall population growth during this period, with 7% in developed countries and 28% in developing countries, but it also reflects the rapid growth of the young population in developing countries.	no
青少年和年轻成年人在吸毒者中所占比例最大。	Adolescents and young adults account for the largest proportion of drug addicts.	no
在2000-2018年期间，发展中国家这一年龄段的人口增长了16%,而发达国家这一年龄段的人口减少了10%。	Between 2000 and 2018, the population of this age group in developing countries increased by 16%, while the population of this age group in developed countries decreased by 10%.	no
1城市化是当前和未来毒品市场的一个驱动因素	1 Urbanization is a driving factor in the current and future drug market	no
无论是发达国家还是发展中国家，城市地区的吸毒情况都多于农村地区。	Whether it is developed or developing countries, drug abuse in urban areas is higher than in rural areas.	no
吸毒情况总体增多的部分原因是人口从农村向城镇的大规模流动一目前全世界人口有一半以上生活在城市地区，而1960年这一比例为34%。	Part of the overall increase in drug abuse is due to the large-scale movement of the population from rural areas to urban areas. At present, more than half of the world's population lives in urban areas, compared with 34% in 1960.	no
城市化可能是毒品市场未来动态的一个关键因素，特别是在城市化趋势更为突出的发展中国家。	Urbanization may be a key factor in the future dynamics of the drug market, especially in developing countries where urbanization trends are more prominent.	no
财富的增加与吸毒情况增多相联，但承受疾病负担最大的是最贫穷的人在世界范围内，发达国家的吸毒情况比发展中国家更为普遍。	The increase in wealth is linked to the increase in drug abuse, but it is the poorest people who bear the greatest burden of disease. Worldwide, drug abuse in developed countries is more common than in developing countries.	no
可卡因之类的毒品更是与世界上较富裕的地区联系较为牢固。	Drugs such as cocaine are more strongly linked to wealthier regions of the world.	no
同样，在各国内部，社会富裕阶层的吸毒流行率较高。	Similarly, within countries, the prevalence of drug abuse among the wealthy strata of society is higher.	no
但转为吸毒病症的比率较高的却是社会经济地位较低的人。	However, it is people of lower socio-economic status who have a higher rate of turning to drug abuse.	no
来自少数几个国家的数据表明，有害的吸毒模式与病症同低收入之间存在联系。	Data from a few countries show that there is a link between harmful drug abuse patterns and illness and low income.	no
这些模式在较富裕的社会阶层似乎不太常见。	These patterns seem to be less common in wealthier social strata.	no
全球新冠肺炎危机造成的经济制约很可能会加剧包括吸毒者在内的最弱势群体的风险。	The economic constraints caused by the global COVID-19 crisis are likely to exacerbate the risks of the most vulnerable groups, including drug addicts.	no
例如，劳动力市场的变化，如失业率上升，过去一直与吸毒情况的增加有关，而这场疫情己经迫使全球数千万人失业。	For example, changes in the labor market, such as rising unemployment, have been related to an increase in drug abuse in the past, and the epidemic has forced tens of millions of people around the world to lose their jobs.	no
新冠肺炎或将导致毒品市场进一步扩张新冠肺炎的大流行可能会导致更多农民增加或从事非法作物种植，或是因为国家主管机关的控制能力降低，或是因为在经济危机之下可能有更多人不得不铤而走险，从事非法活动。	The new crown pneumonia may lead to the further expansion of the drug market. The new crown pneumonia pandemic may cause more farmers to increase or engage in illegal crop cultivation, either because the control capacity of the competent national authorities is reduced, or because under the economic crisis, more people may have to take risks and engage in illegal activities.	no
新冠肺炎的相关限制措施导致空中和陆路交通减少，海上贩运可能已经因此而增加，海上的拦截风险低，而且比空中或陆路走私的数量更多。	The restrictions related to the new crown pneumonia have led to a decrease in air and land traffic, and maritime trafficking may have increased as a result. The risk of interception at sea is low, and there is more smuggling than air or land.	no
最近已有报告称可卡因货物直接从南美经由海路运往欧洲。	Recently, there have been reports that cocaine shipments are shipped directly from South America to Europe by sea.	no
复杂性增强	Increased complexity	yes
非国际管制物质的出现情况稳定，但有潜在危害的新型类阿片正在增多毒品市场正日趋复杂。	The emergence of non-internationally controlled substances is stable, but potentially harmful new types of opioids are increasing, and the drug market is becoming more and more complex.	yes
除大麻、可卡因和海洛因等植物类物质之外，已经增添了数百种合成毒品，其中许多并不在国际管制之下。药品的非医疗使用也快速增多。	In addition to plant-based substances such as cannabis, cocaine and heroin, hundreds of synthetic drugs have been added, many of which are not under international control.The non-medical use of medicines is also increasing rapidly.	yes
会员国的国内市场每年约有500种新型活性物质。	There are about 500 new active substances in the domestic market of Member States every year.	yes
目前其中大多是兴奋剂，其次是合成的大麻素受体激动剂和少量的类阿片。	At present, most of them are stimulants, followed by synthetic cannabinoid receptor agonists and a small amount of opioids.	yes
虽然新型精神活性物质的总体数量已经稳定下来，但比例发生了变化。	Although the overall number of new psychoactive substances has stabilized, the proportion has changed.	yes
在2014年确定的新型精神活性物质种类总数中，类阿片新型精神活性物质仅占2%,但到2018年，这一数字己上升至9%。	Among the total number of new types of psychologically active substances identified in 2014, new types of psychologically active substances such as opioids accounted for only 2%, but by 2018, this number had risen to 9%.	yes
类阿片新型精神活性物质中有许多是芬太尼的类似物，其药效和危害已得到证明，在北美导致了过量死亡事件，其他区域也有，但程度较轻。	Many of the new types of opiate psychoactive substances are analogues of Fentanyl. Their efficacy and harm have been proven to cause overdose deaths in North America, as well as in other regions, but to a lesser extent.	yes
在北美，芬太尼有的用作海洛因和其他毒品（包括可卡因和甲基苯丙胺）的掺杂剂，有的用来制造假冒的药用类阿片。	In North America, fentanyl is used as a dopant for heroin and other drugs (including cocaine and methamphetamine), and some are used to make counterfeit medicinal opioids.	yes
一些证据表明，欧洲也有注射新型精神活性物质兴奋剂的现象：一项对欧洲六个城市废弃注射器残留物的研宄发现，许多注射器都沾有产生兴奋作用的新型精神活性物质》	Some evidence shows that there is also a phenomenon of injecting new psychoactive substance stimulants in Europe: A study of the residues of abandoned syringes in six European cities found that many syringes are stained with new psychoactive substances that produce excitatory effects.	yes
2新型精神活性物质的使用可能会逐渐牢固存在于弱势群体中	2The use of new psychoactive substances may gradually become firmly present in vulnerable groups	no
单一种类的新型精神活性物质几乎从未形成大的市场。	A single type of new psychoactive substance has almost never formed a large market.	no
但来自欧洲的证据表明，合成大麻素在无家可归者和监狱囚犯等社会边缘群体中是一个严重的问题。	But evidence from Europe shows that synthetic cannabinoids are a serious problem in marginalized groups such as the homeless and prison prisoners.	no
有22个国家报告了监狱中使用新型精神活性物质的情况，其中大多数国家将合成大麻素确定为主要挑战。	Twenty-two countries have reported the use of novel psychoactive substances in prisons, and most of them have identified synthetic cannabinoids as the main challenge.	no
对前体化学品的管制迫使制毒者进行创新最常作为前体用来合成苯丙胺、甲基苯丙胺和“摇头丸”等毒品的许多化学品已被置于国际管制之下。	The control of precursor chemicals has forced drug makers to innovate. Many chemicals that are most often used as precursors to synthesize drugs such as amphetamine, methamphetamine, and “ecstasy” have been placed under international control.	no
贩毒者和制毒者一直在寻找替代品一不仅有管制较松的物质，还有专门为规避管制而设计的化学品，即所谓的“特制前体”。	Drug traffickers and drug makers have been looking for alternatives, not only looser controlled substances, but also chemicals specially designed to evade control, the so-called “special precursor”.	no
旨在阻止新冠肺炎传播的限制性措施很可能使依赖前体化学品的制毒者受到进一步挤压。	Restrictive measures aimed at preventing the spread of the new crown pneumonia are likely to further squeeze drug makers who rely on precursor chemicals.	no
来自墨西哥的证据表明，这已经成为 现实：据报告，2020年3月，从东亚进口的甲基苯丙胺前体短缺促使墨西哥和美国的甲基苯丙胺价格上涨。	Evidence from Mexico shows that this has become a reality: in March 2020, it was reported that the shortage of methamphetamine precursor imported from East Asia prompted an increase in the price of methamphetamine in Mexico and the United States.	no
市场瞬息万变	The market is changing rapidly	no
合成药物在中亚和俄罗斯联邦取代阿片剂	Synthetic drugs replace opiate in Central Asia and the Russian Federation	no
中亚和俄罗斯联邦的阿片剂市场在2008年至2018年期间似乎发生了变化。	The opiate market in Central Asia and the Russian Federation seems to have changed between 2008 and 2018.	no
俄罗斯联邦当局截获的阿片剂数量下降了约80%，同时因使用类阿片而接受治疗的人数大幅减少。	The number of opiate intercepts by the authorities of the Russian Federation has fallen by about 80%, while the number of people receiving treatment for the use of opiate has decreased significantly.	no
但兴奋剂市场却似乎日渐兴旺。	But the stimulant market seems to be booming day by day.	no
有证据表明，甲基苯丙胺和各种卡西酮，包括甲氧麻黄酮和 a - 吡咯烷基苯戊酮，现在俄罗斯毒品市场上随处可见。	There is evidence that methamphetamine and various cassidones, including methamphetamine and a-pyrrolidinophenylpentanone, are now everywhere in the Russian drug market.	no
俄罗斯当局报告称，最近查获的制造各种非法药物的秘密加工点数量急剧上升，在两年内翻了一番多，2018年增至152个加工点。	The Russian authorities reported that the number of clandestine processing points for the manufacture of various illegal drugs recently seized has risen sharply, more than doubling in two years and increasing to 152 processing points in 2018.	no
阿富汗和伊拉克甲基苯丙胺市场增长	Growth of the methamphetamine market in Afghanistan and Iraq	no
早在2012年，对医院、监狱和其他机构人员的调查就已经揭示了甲基苯丙胺在伊拉克的重要性。	As early as 2012, investigations of personnel in hospitals, prisons and other institutions have revealed the importance of methamphetamine in Iraq.	no
结晶甲基苯丙胺已经成为“芬乃他林”和曲马多之外又一种令人担忧的主要药物。	Crystallized methamphetamine has become another worrisome major drug in addition to ”fenetalin" and tramadol.	no
2015年的一项研宄进一步证实了这些发现，吸毒者表示大麻比“芬乃他林”或甲基苯丙胺更难获得。	A 2015 study further confirmed these findings, with drug addicts saying that cannabis is more difficult to obtain than “fenetalin” or methamphetamine.	no
最近，伊拉克当局发现了多个甲基苯丙胺加工点，麻管局已对伪麻黄碱制剂的大批进口表示关切一甲基苯丙胺加工点将这些制剂用作前体。	Recently, the Iraqi authorities have discovered a number of methamphetamine processing sites, and the Board has expressed concern about the large-scale import of pseudoephedrine preparations. methylamphetamine processing sites use these preparations as precursors.	no
在阿富汗，甲基苯丙胺制造似乎始于2014年。	In Afghanistan, methamphetamine manufacturing seems to have begun in 2014.	no
自那时起，甲基苯丙胺的缉获量一直在稳步上升。	Since then, methamphetamine seizures have been steadily increasing.	no
但2019年上半年的缉获量一^657公斤——与上一年相比大幅骤增。	However, the seizure volume in the first half of 2019 was 1^657 kg-a sharp increase compared with the previous year.	no
在其他国家大量缉获了据认为源自阿富汗的甲基苯丙胺，这也表明该国的产量正在迅速上升。	A large number of methamphetamine believed to have originated in Afghanistan have been seized in other countries, which also shows that the country's production is rising rapidly.	no
政策变化和变化趋势	Policy changes and trends	yes
非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域大多有大麻使用增多的趋势	Most jurisdictions that legalize non-medical use of cannabis have a trend of increasing cannabis use	yes
加拿大、乌拉圭和美国的11个法域允许制造大麻产品供非医疗使用。	Eleven jurisdictions in Canada, Uruguay, and the United States allow the manufacture of cannabis products for non-medical use.	yes
在其中多数法域，大麻使用自合法化以来有所增多，尽管在其他未将非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域也观察到了同样的趋势。	In most of these jurisdictions, cannabis use has increased since legalization, although the same trend has been observed in other jurisdictions that have not legalized non-medical cannabis use.	yes
在美国最早通过立法的两个州科罗拉多州和华盛顿州，成年人非医疗使用大麻的情况增加，特别是过去一个月以及每天或几乎每天使用的情况增多，自2012年起便已超过了全国平均水平。	In Colorado and Washington State, the two earliest states in the United States to pass legislation, the non-medical use of cannabis by adults has increased, especially in the past month and the increase in daily or almost daily use, which has exceeded the national average since 2012.	yes
所有指标都显示，自2011年以来，乌拉圭的大麻使用情况有所增加，上月使用情况几乎翻了一番。	All indicators show that the use of cannabis in Uruguay has increased since 2011, and the use almost doubled last month.	yes
这表明增加的主要原因是经常和频繁使用大麻。	This indicates that the main reason for the increase is frequent and frequent use of cannabis.	yes
加拿大的短期数据也表明，2018年至2019年合法市场扩大的同时，使用量也在增加。	Short-term data from Canada also show that while the legal market expanded from 2018 to 2019, usage was also increasing.	yes
然而，2019年仍有40%的大麻使用者靠非法来源获得某些产品。	However, in 2019, 40% of cannabis users still relied on illegal sources to obtain certain products.	yes
全球大麻药草缉获量暴跌的背后原因是大麻合法化？	Is the reason behind the plunge in global cannabis herb seizures the legalization of cannabis?	yes
2018年，全球大麻药草缉获量降至20年来的最低水平，这是因为北美的缉获量下降，在过去10年中下降了 84%。	In 2018, global cannabis herb seizures fell to the lowest level in 20 years. This is due to a decline in North American seizures, which have fallen by 84% in the past 10 years.	no
相比之下，同期世界其他地区的缉获量几乎翻了一番。缉获的模式表明，旨在放开大麻市场的政策在下降中发挥了关键作用。	In contrast, seizures in other parts of the world almost doubled during the same period.The pattern of seizures shows that policies aimed at liberalizing the cannabis market have played a key role in the decline.	no
对新型精神活性物质的监管似乎有遏制作用在国内对新型精神活性物质的监管效果仍然很难评估。	The supervision of new psychologically active substances seems to have a curbing effect. The effect of the supervision of new psychologically active substances in China is still difficult to evaluate.	no
一些对新型精神活性物质采用不同监管制度的国家显示出不同的新型精神活性物质使用流行率。	Some countries that adopt different regulatory systems for new psychoactive substances have shown different prevalence rates of the use of new psychoactive substances.	no
在另一些国家，通过国内立法后，新型精神活性物质使用情况有所减少。	In other countries, the use of new psychoactive substances has decreased after the adoption of domestic legislation.	no
弱势群体面临合法和非法毒品市场的伤害用于疼痛管理和姑息治疗的药用类阿片主要在高收入国家提供止痛药在各区域分布不均。	Vulnerable groups face harm from the legal and illegal drug markets. Medicinal opioids used for pain management and palliative care are mainly provided in high-income countries. Painkillers are unevenly distributed in various regions.	no
2018年，所有可供医疗消费的药用类阿片中，90%以上在高收入国家。	In 2018, more than 90% of all medicinal opioids available for medical consumption were in high-income countries.	no
大约50%在北美，40%在欧洲，还有2%在大洋洲。	About 50% are in North America, 40% are in Europe, and 2% are in Oceania.	no
这些国家的人口约占全球人口的12%。	The population of these countries accounts for about 12% of the global population.	no
据估计，低收入和中等收入国家的人口占全球人口的88%,但消费的药用类阿片却不到10%。	It is estimated that the population of low- and middle-income countries accounts for 88% of the global population, but less than 10% of medicinal opioids are consumed.	no
获取药用类阿片的障碍与许多因素有关，包括立法、文化、卫生系统和处方做法。	Barriers to access to medicinal opioids are related to many factors, including legislation, culture, health systems, and prescribing practices.	no
较贫穷的人患吸毒病症的风险更大2018年约有3,560万人患有吸毒病症。	Poorer people are at greater risk of developing drug abuse disorders. In 2018, about 35.6 million people suffered from drug abuse disorders.	no
贫困、有限的教育和社会边缘化可能会增加吸毒病症风险，并加剧其后果。高收入国家的研宄证实了这一点，在这些研究中，个人不利的社会经济轨迹一不仅仅是他们在某一时间点的状况一也与吸毒病症风险有关。	Poverty, limited education, and social marginalization may increase the risk of drug abuse and exacerbate its consequences.Studies in high-income countries have confirmed this. In these studies, the unfavorable socio-economic trajectory of individuals is not only their condition at a certain point in time, but also related to the risk of drug abuse and illness.	no
吸毒病症还会加深社会经济劣势，进一步增加失业、贫困和无家可归的风险，从而助长劣势的恶性循环。这些结果也可能与刑事司法系统内的侮辱性态度和后果有关。	Drug abuse can also deepen socio-economic disadvantage and further increase the risk of unemployment, poverty, and homelessness, thereby fueling a vicious circle of disadvantage.These results may also be related to insulting attitudes and consequences within the criminal justice system.	no
妇女、少数民族和移民、性取向多样化群体、因武装冲突或灾难而流离失所的人以及农村环境中的人也可能受到吸毒病症的过重影响，或者在获得治疗服务方面遇到问题。	Women, ethnic minorities and immigrants, groups with diverse sexual orientations, people displaced by armed conflicts or disasters, and people in rural environments may also be disproportionately affected by drug abuse or encounter problems in accessing treatment services.	no
根据估计因残疾和过早死亡而损失的健康寿命年数的残疾调整寿命年（DALY)指标，在过去10年中，有害的吸毒对范围更广的社会影响加重。	According to the disability-adjusted life expectancy (DALY) index that estimates the number of healthy life expectancy years lost due to disability and premature death, in the past 10 years, harmful drug abuse has had an increased impact on a wider range of society.	no
2007年至2018年间，归因于吸毒的全球残疾调整寿命年数增加了 17%。	Between 2007 and 2018, the global disability-adjusted life span attributable to drug abuse increased by 17%.	no
注射吸毒者中常见的未经治疗的丙型肝炎导致的肝癌的相关残疾调整寿命年数增幅特别高——达到40%。	The increase in disability-adjusted life expectancy for liver cancer caused by untreated hepatitis C, which is common among injecting drug users, is particularly high-reaching 40%.	no
毒品和暴力之间的关系错综复杂很难确定精神活性物质的使用和暴力之间的所有因果关系。	The relationship between drugs and violence is complicated and it is difficult to determine all causal relationships between the use of psychoactive substances and violence.	no
全球范围的有限数据表明，迷醉可能是杀人的一个重要因素。	Limited data on a global scale indicate that intoxication may be an important factor in homicide.	no
但在暴力事件中，酒精的作用似乎比毒品更大。	But in violent incidents, alcohol seems to play a greater role than drugs.	no
虽然吸毒可能会导致犯罪，但在某些情况下，这种联系可以部分归因于多种中介因素，如社会经济劣势以及由个人风险、家庭环境和同龄人影响造成的其他类型的逆境。	Although drug abuse may lead to crime, in some cases, this connection can be partly attributed to a variety of intermediary factors, such as socio-economic disadvantage and other types of adversity caused by personal risk, family environment, and peer influence.	no
贩毒和暴力之间的联系是多方面的。	The link between drug trafficking and violence is multifaceted.	no
如果已有稳定的犯罪结构，包括国际贩毒在内的大规模有组织犯罪活动有可能在无暴力的情况下实施。	If there is a stable criminal structure, large-scale organized criminal activities, including international drug trafficking, may be carried out without violence.	no
短期内，暴力的存在和程度与其说取决于贩运的数量，不如说取决于造成有组织犯罪集团之间力量平衡不稳定的某些变化，例如非法市场规模的变化，知名罪犯的死亡或监禁，以及使一个集团弱于另一个集团的执法措施。	In the short term, the existence and extent of violence depends not so much on the amount of trafficking as on certain changes that cause instability in the balance of power between organized criminal groups, such as changes in the size of the illegal market, the death or imprisonment of well-known criminals, and law enforcement measures that make one group weaker than another.	no
最新趋势	Latest trends	yes
吸毒大麻是最常用的物质，类阿片危害最大	Cannabis is the most commonly used substance for drug use, and opioids are the most harmful	yes
据估计，2018年使用大麻的有 1.92 亿人，使之成为全球使用最多的毒品。	It is estimated that 192 million people used cannabis in 2018, making it the most used drug in the world.	yes
相比之下，2018年使用类阿片的有5,800万人。	In contrast, there were 58 million people who used opioids in 2018.	yes
但阿片类药物的相关危害却因使用者较少而受到忽视。	However, the related harms of opioids are ignored because there are fewer users.	yes
在2017年与吸毒病症有关的估计167,000例死亡中，有66%是这类物质造成的，在据信为吸毒导致的残疾或过早死亡而损失的2,100万年寿命中，有50%是这类物质造成的。	Of the estimated 167,000 deaths related to drug abuse in 2017, 66% were caused by such substances, and 50% of the 21 million life span believed to have been lost due to disability or premature death caused by drug abuse was caused by such substances.	yes
合成类阿片的非医疗使用加剧了公共卫生危机	The non-medical use of synthetic opioids has exacerbated the public health crisis	yes
在西非、中部非洲和北非，加剧类阿片危机的是曲马多；在北美则是芬太尼。这两个区域在经济、人口统计数据或一般吸毒模式方面几乎没有共同点，但都在奋力抗击由容易获得且生产成本低的物质助长的类阿片危机。	In West Africa, Central Africa, and North Africa, tramadol is exacerbating the opioid crisis; in North America, it is fentanyl.The two regions have little in common in terms of economy, demographic statistics, or general drug abuse patterns, but they are both struggling to combat the opioid crisis driven by easily available and low-cost substances.	yes
在北美，芬太尼等合成类阿片的使用导致了20年来类阿片过量致死人数增加。	In North America, the use of synthetic opioids such as fentanyl has led to an increase in the number of deaths from opioid overdoses in the past 20 years.	yes
2018年，在美国登记的67,367例过量死亡中，有三分之二涉及芬太尼。	In 2018, two-thirds of the 67,367 overdose deaths registered in the United States involved fentanyl.	yes
加拿大也报告了类似的结果，只是数字较低。	Canada also reported similar results, but the number is lower.	no
芬太尼导致过量死亡的部分原因是非法药物市场上的芬太尼药效不可预测。	Part of the reason for overdose deaths caused by fentanyl is the unpredictable efficacy of fentanyl on the illegal drug market.	no
在西非、中部非洲和北非，非医疗用途曲马多的市场已有大幅增长。	In West Africa, Central Africa and North Africa, the market for tramadol for non-medical purposes has grown significantly.	no
在该区域，接受治疗的曲马多使用病症患者越来越多。	In this region, more and more patients with tramadol use disorders are receiving treatment.	no
2017年，全球截获的曲马多数量显著增加，达到125吨以上的峰值。	In 2017, the number of tramadol intercepted worldwide increased significantly, reaching a peak of more than 125 tons.	no
但2018年，在印度通过一项监管曲马多的新法律之后，全球缉获量降至32吨。	But in 2018, after India passed a new law regulating tramadol, global seizures fell to 32 tons.	no
促成这两地危机的是制造简单和生产成本低，此外还有对曲马多和许多芬太尼类似物或其前体缺乏国际监管。	What contributed to the crises in these two places was the simplicity of manufacturing and low production costs, in addition to the lack of international regulation of tramadol and many fentanyl analogues or their precursors.	no
使这两地危机恶化的是这些物质在药品市场和非法市场上都有供应，因而更加难以发现和防止其滥用。	What makes the crisis in these two places worse is that these substances are available in both the drug market and the illegal market, making it more difficult to detect and prevent their abuse.	no
兴奋剂使用不断增多	The use of stimulants is increasing	no
兴奋剂领域以可卡因和甲基苯丙胺为主，这两种物质在其主要市场的使用量都在上升。	The field of stimulants is dominated by cocaine and methamphetamine, and the use of these two substances in their main markets is on the rise.	no
2018年使用可卡因的约有1,900万人，因为可卡因在北美和西欧颇为流行。	About 19 million people used cocaine in 2018, because cocaine is quite popular in North America and Western Europe.	no
同年使用苯丙胺的约有2,700万人，其中甲基苯丙胺是东南亚和北美使用最多的苯丙胺类兴奋剂。	In the same year, about 27 million people used amphetamines, of which methamphetamine was the most used amphetamine-type stimulant in Southeast Asia and North America.	no
根据所掌握的多数指标，20年来这两个区域甲基苯丙胺的使用一直在扩大。	According to most indicators available, the use of methamphetamine in these two regions has been expanding for 20 years.	no
在一些市场上，可卡因和甲基苯丙胺可以共存，有时是相互替代，这样一种药物的使用量上升时另一种药物的使用量就下降，有时是同时增加和减少以满足同一市场的需求。	In some markets, cocaine and methamphetamine can coexist, sometimes replacing each other, so that when the use of one drug rises, the use of the other drops, sometimes increasing and decreasing at the same time to meet the demand of the same market.	no
新冠肺炎使注射吸毒者的风险增高	New crown pneumonia increases the risk of injecting drug users	no
据估计，2018年注射吸毒的约有1,130万人，全球艾滋病毒感染约有10%是注射吸毒造成的。	It is estimated that there were about 11.3 million people who used injecting drugs in 2018, and about 10% of global HIV infections were caused by injecting drugs.	no
注射吸毒者感染艾滋病毒的超过100万人，患丙型肝炎的有550万人。	There are more than 1 million people infected with HIV by injecting drug users and 5.5 million people suffering from hepatitis C.	no
2017年，因吸毒死亡的约有 58.5万人，其中一半死于丙型肝炎引起的肝病，而注射吸毒者的丙型肝炎大多仍未得到治疗。	In 2017, there were about 585,000 deaths due to drug abuse, half of which died of liver disease caused by hepatitis C, and most of the hepatitis C of injecting drug users has still not been treated.	no
5 新冠肺炎限制措施造成的类阿片短缺可能导致使用者代之以酒精或苯二氮类药物等更容易获得的物质，或者将类阿片与合成药物混合。	5The shortage of opioids caused by the restrictive measures of the new crown pneumonia may cause users to replace more readily available substances such as alcohol or benzodiazepines, or mix opioids with synthetic drugs.	no

欧盟峰会为难民政策争论，欧盟官员：接收过程步步瓶颈-中新网	The EU summit is in a difficult policy debate, EU officials: The receiving process is a bottleneck step by step- <url>	yes
欧盟峰会为难民政策争吵不休，欧盟官员：接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈	The EU summit quarreled over refugee policy endlessly. EU officials: There are bottlenecks at every step of the reception process.	yes
【环球时报驻比利时特派记者 牛瑞飞】据法新社2月10日报道，在当天最新的一次欧盟峰会上，欧盟委员会主席冯德莱恩表示，欧盟领导人同意就非法移民问题出台更严格的政策，以此更易于驱逐非法移民。	[Niu Ruifei, special correspondent of the Global Times in Belgium] According to a report by Agence France-Presse on February 10, at the latest EU summit that day, European Commission President Von der Leyen said that EU leaders agreed to introduce stricter policies on illegal immigration to make it easier to expel illegal immigrants.	yes
据报道，欧盟此举是对欧洲日益增长的非法移民问题关注的回应，如今，欧盟的核心问题在于，最终能被遣返的非法移民人数很少。	According to reports, the EU's move is a response to Europe's growing concern about illegal immigration. Today, the core problem of the EU is that the number of illegal immigrants who can eventually be returned is very small.	yes
根据峰会文件，欧盟领导人呼吁委员会“立即调动大量欧盟资金”，以基础设施和监视等手段加强外部边界。	According to the summit document, EU leaders called on the Commission to “immediately mobilize a large amount of EU funds” to strengthen external borders through infrastructure and surveillance.	yes
然而，欧盟与各成员国就围栏费用支付等问题争吵不休。	However, the EU and member states quarreled endlessly on issues such as the payment of fence fees.	yes
冯德莱恩一再表示，欧盟资金不会支付相关费用。	Von der Leyen has repeatedly stated that EU funds will not pay for related expenses.	yes
但一些成员国的外交官员称，如果欧盟能分担外部边界沿线安装摄像头、瞭望塔和其他基础设施的部分，这将给各国腾出国家预算从而加快建设进程。	But diplomats from some member states said that if the EU can share the cost of installing cameras, watchtowers and other infrastructure along its external borders, it will free up national budgets for countries to speed up the construction process.	yes
欧洲Euractiv网站称，欧盟官员承认，难民接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈，有限的接收能力和成员国不堪重负的移民当局无法阻止难民在欧盟各国提交“无数”庇护申请，欧盟的难民接收系统处于近乎“永久性的危机”中。	According to the European Euractivity website, EU officials admit that there are bottlenecks at every step of the refugee reception process. The limited reception capacity and the overwhelmed immigration authorities of member states cannot prevent refugees from submitting “countless” asylum applications in EU countries, and the EU's refugee reception system is in an almost “permanent crisis.”	yes
据欧盟委员会估计，欧盟的申根国家去年收到超92万份庇护申请，比前一年增加近半。	According to estimates by the European Commission, the EU's Schengen countries received more than 920,000 asylum applications last year, an increase of nearly half over the previous year.	yes
与此同时，欧盟去年记录到超 33万次非法入境。	At the same time, the European Union recorded more than 330,000 illegal entries last year.	no
在该背景下，此次峰会还就一项“原则”达成协议，即欧盟国家可根据另一个成员国的法院判决将非法移民遣返回国。	In this context, the summit also reached an agreement on a “principle” that EU countries can return illegal immigrants to their countries in accordance with a court decision of another member state.	no
此外，报道称，欧盟领导人还同意“增加对安全国家概念的使用”，这将为欧盟制定共同清单开辟道路。	In addition, the report said that EU leaders also agreed to “increase the use of the concept of a safe country,” which will open the way for the EU to develop a common list.	no

美国升级“芯片战”重创全球半导体产业-中新网	The U.S. upgrades the "chip war” and hits the global semiconductor industry hard- <url>	yes
最近，美国对华“芯片战”大有升级之势——先是荷兰、日本两国在美国施压下，同意启动对华半导体制造设备出口的管制；后有外媒报道，美国政府正考虑切断美国供应商与华为公司之间的所有联系，禁止美国供应商向华为提供任何产品；拜登政府还准备公布一项行政命令，限制美国对敏感的中国科技行业的投资……2023年开年不久，美国在遏制中国半导体相关产业发展上就恶招不断。	Recently, the “chip war” between the United States and China has greatly upgraded-first, the Netherlands and Japan, under pressure from the United States, agreed to initiate controls on the export of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China; later, foreign media reported that the U.S. government is considering cutting off all ties between U.S. suppliers and Huawei and prohibiting U.S. suppliers from providing any products to Huawei; the Biden administration is also preparing to announce an executive order to restrict U.S. investment in sensitive Chinese technology industries...Soon after the start of the new year in 2023, the United States will continue to make bad moves in curbing the development of China's semiconductor-related industries.	yes
近年来，美国打击中国“芯”发展的动作从未停歇，一边精准打压对华半导体产供链，一边构建“去中国化”的半导体产业链联盟，图谋在先进半导体产业上彻底“甩开”中国。	In recent years, the United States has never stopped its actions to combat the development of China's “core”. While accurately suppressing the semiconductor production and supply chain to China, it has built a “de-sinicized” semiconductor industry chain alliance, aiming to completely “get rid” of China in the advanced semiconductor industry. China.	yes
无论是拉拢韩国建立“技术同盟”，还是与韩国、日本和中国台湾地区建立芯片“四方联盟”，亦或借由美日印澳“四边机制”“印太经济框架”等机制建立半导体产业链“小圈子”，美国通过把政治化、阵营化、武器化的手段引入半导体产业，企图搭建美国主导的封闭产供链循环，从而弥补其在芯片制造领域的短板，维护其在全球芯片产业的优势地位。	Whether it is to win over South Korea to establish a “technological alliance”, to establish a chip “quartet alliance” with South Korea, Japan, and Taiwan, China, or to establish a “small circle” of the semiconductor industry chain through mechanisms such as the “four-sided mechanism” of the United States, Japan, India and Australia, and the “Indo-Pacific Economic Framework”, the United States has introduced politicization, campization, and weaponization into the semiconductor industry in an attempt to build a closed production and supply chain cycle led by the United States, thereby making up for its shortcomings in the field of chip manufacturing and maintaining its dominant position in the global chip industry.	yes
然而，美国大张旗鼓的对华“芯战术”，也是“伤敌一千自损八百”。	However, the “core tactics” of the United States against China with great fanfare are also “hurting the enemy by one thousand and self-harming by eight hundred.”	yes
最近，美国知名芯片制造设备供应商泛林集团宣布，受最新一轮对华芯片制造设备出口禁令影响，集团将解雇1300名全职员工，未来两个季度还计划解雇1400名临时员工。	Recently, Panlin Group, a well-known chip manufacturing equipment supplier in the United States, announced that due to the latest round of export bans on chip manufacturing equipment to China, the group will lay off 1,300 full-time employees, and plans to lay off 1,400 temporary employees in the next two quarters.	yes
全球光刻机巨头荷兰阿斯麦控股公司最近警告，禁止向中国出口半导体制造设备，可能导致半导体价格上涨。	The global lithography machine giant Asma Holding Company of the Netherlands recently warned that a ban on the export of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China may lead to higher semiconductor prices.	yes
美媒分析，在美国政府对中国芯片和半导体等行业实施蛮横打压后，许多美国公司深受其害，包括电子设计自动化工具开发商、芯片设计商、晶圆制造设备生产商、芯片制造商本身等。	According to US media analysis, after the US government implemented an outrageous crackdown on China's chip and semiconductor industries, many American companies have suffered greatly, including electronic design automation tool developers, chip designers, wafer manufacturing equipment manufacturers, chip manufacturers themselves, etc.	yes
美国所谓打压中国先进半导体产业，却把全球半导体产业链、供应链拖下了水。	The so-called suppression of China's advanced semiconductor industry by the United States has dragged the global semiconductor industry chain and supply chain down.	yes
半导体产业是高技术和知识密集型产业，早已形成联系紧密的全球半导体产业链。	The semiconductor industry is a high-tech and knowledge-intensive industry, and a closely linked global semiconductor industry chain has long been formed.	yes
据专业人士估算，基于专业化分工，半导体产品的整个生产过程需要跨越各国边境70次以上，全程达到100天。	According to professional estimates, based on the professional division of labor, the entire production process of semiconductor products needs to cross the borders of various countries more than 70 times, and the whole process reaches 100 days.	no
尽管美国半导体产业基础较强，但在制造能力特别是先进制程工艺上较为薄弱，严重依赖东亚地区。	Although the U.S. semiconductor industry has a strong foundation, it is relatively weak in manufacturing capabilities, especially advanced process technology, and relies heavily on East Asia.	no
即便美国极力引导先进芯片产供链转向美国主导的“小圈子”区域化发展，但全球半导体相关产业的地区分布和相互依赖局面很难被改变。	Even if the United States tries its best to guide the advanced chip production and supply chain to the regionalization of the “small circle” led by the United States, the regional distribution and interdependence of the global semiconductor-related industries are difficult to change.	no
美国强力“重塑”“去中国化”的半导体产业链，重创全球半导体产业。	The United States has vigorously "reshaped” and "de-sinicized" the semiconductor industry chain, which has hit the global semiconductor industry hard.	no
芯片是全球未来产业的核心，芯片产业的发展离不开全球各国共同参与。	Chips are the core of the global future industry, and the development of the chip industry is inseparable from the joint participation of countries around the world.	no
近年来，美国采取一系列单边行动，相继出台《创新与竞争法案》《2022年美国竞争法案》《芯片和科学法案》，利用科技霸权，巩固本国技术领先优势；对盟友“恩威并施”，诱逼英特尔、台积电、三星等芯片制造企业赴美设厂，极力确保美国在芯片领域的全球领导地位。	In recent years, the United States has taken a series of unilateral actions, successively introducing the “Innovation and Competition Act”, "U.S. Competition Act of 2022" and "Chip and Science Act" to take advantage of technological hegemony and consolidate its own technological leadership; "Enmity and coercion" to its allies, inducing Intel, TSMC, Samsung and other chip manufacturing companies to set up factories in the United States, and strive to ensure the United States' global leadership in the chip field.	no
短期看，美国确实给中国的芯片产业及相关产业发展制造了麻烦，收获了现实利益。	In the short term, the United States has indeed caused trouble for the development of China's chip industry and related industries, and has reaped real benefits.	no
但长期看，美国歇斯底里地打压，倒逼中国芯片产业不断突破，让自己失去了巨大的中国市场，最终会极大削弱美国科技企业的创新意愿和创新能力，损害全球芯片产业发展。	However, in the long run, the United States has suppressed hysterically, forcing the Chinese chip industry to continue to break through, causing itself to lose the huge Chinese market, which will eventually greatly weaken the innovation willingness and innovation ability of American technology companies, and harm the development of the global chip industry.	no

2月10日，中国理财网发布首批个人养老金理财产品名单，工银理财、农银理财和中邮理财的7只个人养老金理财产品正式发售。	On February 10th, <url> released the list of the first batch of personal pension wealth management products, and seven personal pension wealth management products of ICBC Financial Management, ABCI Financial Management and China Post Financial Management were officially launched.	yes
至此，个人养老金账户的“货架”终于集齐个人养老金储蓄、个人养老金理财、个人养老金保险、个人养老金公募基金四类产品。	At this point, the “shelves” of personal pension accounts have finally gathered four types of products: personal pension savings, personal pension financial management, personal pension insurance, and personal pension public fund.	yes
据介绍，首批个人养老金理财产品，全部为公募类净值型开放式产品，其中新发产品5只、存续产品2只，除1只产品为混合类产品外，其余6只产品均为固定收益类产品。	According to reports, the first batch of personal pension wealth management products are all public equity-type open-ended products, including 5 newly issued products and 2 surviving products. Except for 1 product, which is a mixed product, the remaining 6 products are all fixed income products.	yes
北京青年报记者看到，5只新发产品中有4只来自工银理财，全部是固定收益类产品，最短持有期限分别为365天、540天、720天和1080天，对应的业绩比较基准(年化)分别为3.70 % - 4.20 % 、 4.10 % - 4.60 % 、 4.40 % - 4.90 % 、 5.25 % - 5.75 % 。	Reporters from Beijing Youth Daily saw that 4 of the 5 newly issued products came from ICBC Financial Management, all of which were fixed income products. The minimum holding periods were 365 days, 540 days, 720 days and 1080 days, respectively, and the corresponding performance comparison benchmarks (annualized) were 3.70 % - 4.20 % 、 4.10 % - 4.60 % 、 4.40 % - 4.90 % 、 5.25 % - 5.75 % 。	yes
剩余一只新发产品是“邮银财富添颐·鸿锦最短持有1095 天 1 号 ” ， 也是固定收益类产品，2月10日开始募集，2月19日结束募集，风险等级为二级。	The remaining newly issued product is "Postbank Wealth Tianyi*Hongjin Minimum Holding No. 1 for 1095 Days"” which is also a fixed income product. It began to be raised on February 10 and ended on February 19. The risk level is Level 2.	yes

The cumulative net worth on February 8 was 1.0011.	no
根据《国务院办公厅关于推动个人养老金发展的意见 》 ， 个人养老金资金账户资金可投资的金融产品包括银行理财、储蓄存款、商业养老保险、公募基金等。	According to the "Opinions of the General Office of the State Council on Promoting the Development of Personal Pensions", the financial products that can be invested in personal pension fund accounts include bank wealth management, savings deposits, commercial pension insurance, public equity funds, etc.	no
首批个人养老金理财产品发售，标志着个人养老金投资者可正式通过个人养老金资金账户购买理财产品。	The first batch of personal pension wealth management products are on sale, marking that personal pension investors can officially purchase wealth management products through personal pension fund accounts.	no
去年11月银保监会制定了《商业银行和理财公司个人养老金业务管理暂行办法 》 。	In November last year, the China Banking and Insurance Regulatory Commission formulated the "Interim Measures for the Management of Personal Pension Business of Commercial Banks and Wealth Management Companies".	no
《办法》规定，参加人可以通过个人养老金资金账户购买个人养老储蓄、个人养老金理财产品、个人养老金保险产品、个人养老金公募基金产品等个人养老金产品。	The "Measures" stipulate that participants can purchase personal pension savings, personal pension wealth management products, personal pension insurance products, personal pension public fund products and other personal pension products through their personal pension fund accounts.	no
随后，人社部、财政部、国家税务总局三部门发布通知，明确个人养老金制度在北京、天津，以及河北石家庄、雄安新区，山西晋城市等36个先行城市和地区启动实施。	Subsequently, the three departments of the Ministry of Human Resources and Social Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, and the State Administration of Taxation issued a notice clarifying that the personal pension system will be implemented in 36 leading cities and regions such as Beijing and Tianjin, as well as Shijiazhuang, Xiong'an New District, Hebei, and Jincheng City, Shanxi.	no
截至2022年底，个人养老金参加人数1954万人，缴费人数613万人，总缴费金额142亿元。	By the end of 2022, the number of participants in personal pensions was 19.54 million, the number of contributors was 6.13 million, and the total contribution amount was 14.2 billion yuan.	no
此前，参与试点的银行只上架了个人养老储蓄、个人养老金保险产品和个人养老金公募基金三类产品。	Previously, the banks participating in the pilot only listed three types of products: personal pension savings, personal pension insurance products, and personal pension public funds.	no
如今，个人养老金理财产品也聚齐之后，投资者该如何选择？	Nowadays, after personal pension wealth management products are also gathered, how should investors choose?	no
交银理财产品研发部专家表示，相比其他个人养老金产品，试点阶段的养老理财产品和个人养老金理财产品均具有三方面的特点。	Experts from the Research and Development department of Wealth management products of the Bank of Communications said that compared with other personal pension products, the pension wealth management products and personal pension wealth management products in the pilot phase have three characteristics.	no
一是稳健性，风险管理机制更加健全，投资策略和理念更为稳健，并实施非母行第三方独立托管。	First, robustness, a more sound risk management mechanism, a more robust investment strategy and philosophy, and the implementation of independent escrow by a third party other than the parent bank.	no
二是长期性，试点阶段养老理财产品的期限都在5年及以上，下一步发行的个人养老金理财产品，最短持有期原则上为1年，鼓励持有3年以上。	The second is the long-term nature. The term of pension wealth management products in the pilot phase is 5 years and above. In principle, the minimum holding period for personal pension wealth management products issued in the next step is 1 year, and it is encouraged to hold for more than 3 years.	no
三是普惠性，产品购买门槛低，起购点一般为1元，有的低至0.01元，产品的托管费、管理费等费率更加优惠。	The third is universality. The threshold for product purchase is low. The starting point of purchase is generally 1 yuan, and some are as low as 0.01 yuan. The escrow fee, management fee and other rates of the product are more favorable.	no
专业人士指出，投资者要根据产品特点和自己的风险承受能力进行选择。	Professionals pointed out that investors should choose based on product characteristics and their own risk tolerance.	no
个人养老金储蓄具有期限较长、利率较高、安全性高的特点，适合风险承受能力弱的人群；个人养老金保险产品重在保障，比较适合无法承担投资风险，可以接受稳定收益的人群；而个人养老金理财产品和公募基金产品不保本也不保收益，有一定投资风险，但预期收益较高，适合具备一定的金融知识、风险承担能力较高的人群。	Personal pension savings have the characteristics of long maturity, high interest rates, and high security, and are suitable for people with weak risk tolerance; personal pension insurance products focus on protection, which is more suitable for people who cannot bear investment risks and can accept stable returns; and personal pension wealth management products and public fund products do not protect capital or income, there is a certain investment risk, but the expected return is higher, and it is suitable for people with certain financial knowledge and high risk-taking ability.	no

健身行业应摆脱信任危机-中新网	The fitness industry should get rid of the crisis of trust- <url>	yes

近日，知名健身机构中健健身会员维权问题引起社会关注。	Recently, the issue of rights protection of members of Zhongjian Fitness, a well-known fitness institution, has attracted social attention.	yes
春节后不少会员发现自己所在门店没有正常营业，随后，关于该机构倒闭跑路的传闻引起会员恐慌，导致公安、人社部门介入。	After the Spring Festival, many members found that their stores were not open normally. Subsequently, rumors about the closure of the organization caused panic among members, leading to the intervention of the public security and human resources departments.	yes
最后，该机构相关负责人出面回应，承诺会努力保障好员工和会员的合法权益，风波才得以平息。	Finally, the relevant person in charge of the organization responded and promised to work hard to protect the legitimate rights and interests of employees and members before the storm could subside.	yes
个别健身机构的部分门店出现经营问题，暂时关闭，消费者本可心平气和等待问题解决，为何不少会员的第一反应是“大事不妙”？	Some stores of individual fitness institutions had operating problems and were temporarily closed. Consumers could have calmed down and waited for the problem to be resolved. Why did many members' first reaction be “Something is wrong”?	yes

国内传统健身房普遍采取预付费模式，“赚用户不来的钱”是其发展的底层逻辑。	Traditional domestic gyms generally adopt a prepaid model, and “making money that users can't get” is the underlying logic of their development.	yes
通过预售会员卡获取现金流，不断开新店，看似能够循环往复，实则寅吃卯粮，无法形成稳定的盈利模式。	Obtaining cash flow through pre-sale membership cards and constantly opening new stores seems to be able to cycle back and forth, but in fact, it is impossible to form a stable profit model.	yes
健身房跑路等行业负面信息频频传出，对消费者信心造成强烈冲击。	Negative information in industries such as gym running away frequently spreads, which has a strong impact on consumer confidence.	yes
从市场前景看，健身房当然算得上是一门有“钱途”的好生意。	From the perspective of market prospects, gyms are of course a good business with a “money path”.	no
健身赛道虽然起起伏伏，但始终受到资本关注。	Although the fitness track has ups and downs, it has always received capital attention.	no
多项数据显示，文体消费等领域热度不断攀升，市场持续回暖。	A number of data show that the popularity of cultural and sports consumption and other fields continues to rise, and the market continues to pick up.	no
具体到健身市场，随着居民生活水平稳步提高，健康生活理念深入人心，健身行业发展大有可为。	Specific to the fitness market, with the steady improvement of residents' living standards and the concept of healthy living deeply rooted in the hearts of the people, the development of the fitness industry has great potential.	no
形势越是趋好，行业越需重视发展质量。	The better the situation, the more the industry needs to pay attention to the quality of development.	no
然而，个别机构对消费复苏后的健身市场盲目乐观，刚从危机中走出来，又吹响开疆拓土的号角，把融资资金一股脑投入新店建设上。	However, individual institutions are blindly optimistic about the fitness market after the consumer recovery. As soon as they came out of the crisis, they sounded the horn of expanding their territory and invested their financing funds in the construction of new stores.	no
不可否认，这几年受疫情影响，不少机构退出，行业重新洗牌，有实力的企业此时选择性地加大收购力度、重新布局，未尝不是新机遇。	It is undeniable that in recent years, affected by the epidemic, many institutions have withdrawn and the industry has been reshuffled. It is not a new opportunity for powerful companies to selectively increase their acquisitions and re-layout at this time.	no
但是，健身市场发展要想进入良性循环，迈上行稳致远的康庄大道，行业就必须改变传统模式，改变经营策略。	However, if the development of the fitness market is to enter a virtuous circle and embark on a stable and far-reaching road to prosperity, the industry must change its traditional model and change its business strategy.	no
只有稳扎稳打，重新建立起消费者的信任度、安全感，才能真正赢得市场、赢得未来。	Only by fighting steadily and re-establishing consumer trust and security can we truly win the market and the future.	no
相比大建新店抢占市场，健身行业当前更需要的是沉下心来优化服务，用高质量发展来稳住用户。	Compared with Dajian Xindian to seize the market, what the fitness industry currently needs is to calm down and optimize services, and stabilize users with high-quality development.	no
首先，要靠服务留住用户。	First of all, we must rely on services to retain users.	no
健身房属于服务行业，其本质是坚持“用户导向”，要紧紧围绕用户需求，把经营重心放在服务提质升级上。	Gyms belong to the service industry. Their essence is to adhere to “user-oriented”, closely focus on user needs, and focus on service quality improvement and upgrading.	no
其次，要靠数字化转型提升用户体验。	Secondly, it is necessary to rely on digital transformation to improve the user experience.	no
比如当下流行的互联网健身房模式，实现用户按次付费和场地自选。	For example, the current popular Internet gym model realizes user pay-per-view and venue selection.	no
同时，身体数据、运动数据得以有效利用，还可以满足社交需求，实现从线上到线下完整的服务闭环。	At the same time, body data and exercise data can be effectively used, and social needs can be met, and a complete closed loop of services from online to offline can be realized.	no
没有私教推销，没有巨额年卡，用户对健身机构“跑路”的担忧降低了，信任感也就提升了。	There is no private education promotion and no huge annual card. Users' concerns about fitness institutions “running away” are reduced, and their sense of trust is increased.	no
另外，还要积极探索多元业态。	In addition, we must actively explore multiple formats.	no

买贵退差价！	Buy expensive and refund the difference!	yes
南京楼市再现“差价赔付”-中新网	Nanjing's property market reproduces “price difference compensation”- <url>	yes
扬子晚报讯(记者 马祚波)扬子晚报/紫牛新闻记者10日在采访中发现，十余年未见的“保价协议”又重回了南京楼市，位于江北新区的一家楼盘宣称“差价赔付”，在交房前其他房源的优惠大于之前的折扣，开发商愿意为买房人换房并退还差价。	Yangtze Evening News (Reporter Ma Zuobo) Yangtze Evening News/Zin Niu News reporter found in an interview on the 10th that the “price guarantee agreement” that has not been seen for more than ten years has returned to the Nanjing property market. A real estate in Jiangbei New District claims “price difference compensation”. Before the delivery of the house, the discount of other listings is greater than the previous discount, and the developer is willing to exchange the house for the buyer and refund the difference.	yes
“保价协议”条件可不少	There are many conditions for the "Price guarantee agreement”	yes
这家位于江北新区的楼盘名为保利扬子萃云台，看房人孙先生告诉记者，他在上周末逛楼盘时发现了一则“声明”。	This real estate in Jiangbei New District is called Poly Yangzi Cuiyuntai. The buyer, Mr. Sun, told reporters that he found a “statement” when he visited the real estate last weekend.	yes
他发给记者的图片上显示，该楼盘的开发商承诺，凡是在2月1日-2月28日期间购买房源的，自双方签订买卖合同之日起至对应房源交付，若该项目其他房源的优惠折扣大于之前购房所享折扣的(限与该商品房属于同一户型、同一楼栋、同一单元、同一物业类型的其他未售商品房)，开发商可以为购房者换房并退还差价。	The picture he sent to reporters shows that the developer of the real estate promised that anyone who purchases a listing from February 1st to February 28th will be delivered to the corresponding listing from the date of signing the sale and purchase contract between the two parties. If the discount of other listings in the project is greater than the discount enjoyed by the previous purchase (limited to other unsold commercial properties of the same type, the same building, the same unit, and the same property type as the commercial house), the developer can exchange the house for the buyer and refund the difference.	yes
孙先生表示，置业顾问表示这其实就是一份“保价协议”，目的是让买家放心出手，不用担心开发企业降价促销，“现在就怕买完了它就降价了，去售楼处闹吧没时间，不闹的话也确实窝心”。	Mr. Sun said that the real estate consultant said that this is actually a "price guarantee agreement”. The purpose is to let buyers rest assured that they don't have to worry about the price reduction and promotion of the development company. “Now I'm afraid that the price will be reduced after buying it. Go to the sales office and make trouble. There is no time. If you don't make trouble, it's really sweet.”	yes
还有不少买房人则认为，“保价协议”虽然是在给购房者吃“定心丸”，不过条件却不低。	There are also many buyers who believe that although the “price guarantee agreement” is giving buyers “peace of mind”, the conditions are not low.	yes
打算在江北买一套刚需房的郑女士说，保价的房源首先是要同一户型，还得在同一楼栋、同一个单元，买家可以比价的房源寥寥，因此“门槛”还是蛮高的。	Ms. Zheng, who plans to buy a newly needed house in Jiangbei, said that the insured listing first needs the same apartment type, but also in the same building and the same unit. There are very few listings where buyers can compare prices, so the “threshold” is still quite high.	yes
也有购房者认为，由于信息不对称，销售时不排除给出额外的让利，买家“维权”的难度不小。	Some buyers also believe that due to the asymmetry of information, additional concessions are not ruled out when selling, and it is not difficult for buyers to “defend their rights”.	yes
能否留住买房人有待观察	Whether it can retain buyers remains to be seen	no
记者在南京网上房地产上查询得知，该楼盘于去年11月首领两幢楼共计252套房源的销许，户型面积有105平方米、114平方米、129平方米等，全装修销许均价为39843元/㎡。	The reporter inquired on Nanjing online real estate and learned that the real estate received a total of 252 sales permits for the two buildings in November last year. The apartment area is 105 square meters, 114 square meters, 129 square meters, etc., and the average price of the fully renovated sales permit is 39,843 yuan/㎡.	no
不过两个多月过去，网上房地产显示目前该楼盘的未售总套数为157套，占比为62.3%，其中8号楼共计128套，未售套数达113套，7号楼的124套中也有44套未售，项目的总成交套数只有33套，占比仅为13%。	However, more than two months later, online real estate shows that the total number of unsold units in the real estate is currently 157, accounting for 62.3%. Among them, there are 128 units in Building 8, and the number of unsold units is 113. Of the 124 units in Building 7, 44 are unsold, and the total number of units sold in the project is only 33, accounting for only 13%.	no
市场人士介绍，“保价协议”在2008年也曾在南京出现过。	According to market sources, the “price guarantee agreement” also appeared in Nanjing in 2008.	no
当年8月份，河西黄山路上的楼盘横塘西苑为了吸引买房人眼球，推出了《保价计划》，具体内容为“公司郑重承诺，若一年内项目优惠幅度扩大，由此产生的差额，公司将按差额退还给老业主”。	In August of that year, Hengtang Xiyuan, a real estate on Huangshan Road, Hexi, launched a “Price Guarantee Plan” in order to attract the attention of buyers. The specific content is "The company solemnly promises that if the project discount is expanded within one year, the company will refund the difference to the old owner according to the difference."	no
此后2011年4月，南京也有9家楼盘拿出部分房源承诺“差价赔付”。	Since then, in April 2011, nine real estate companies in Nanjing have also taken out some of their listings and promised to “pay the difference.”	no
“楼市在回暖，此时更需要一针‘强心剂’。	“The property market is picking up, and a ‘tonic’ is needed at this time.	no

其中，蔬菜价格飞涨28.25%，创17个月新高。	Among them, vegetable prices soared by 28.25%, a 17-month high.	no

2022年回国求职应届留学生留学国前10 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	The top 10 pictures of fresh international students returning to China for job search in 2022 Source: "2022 China Returnee Employment Survey Report"	yes
中新网北京2月11日电 (门睿)近日发布的《2022中国海归就业调查报告》(下称“报告”)显示，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高，我国企业对海外人才的需求亦呈上扬态势。	<url>, Beijing, February 11 (Menrui) The recently released “2022 China Returnee Employment Survey Report” (hereinafter referred to as the "Report") shows that the scale of fresh international students in 2022 increased by 8.6% year-on-year, and the number of international students returning to China for job search hit a new high. The demand for overseas talents by Chinese companies is also on the rise.	yes
报告指出，自2020年以来，在中国国内求职的海归数量明显增长，回国求职的应届留学生数量增多。	The report points out that since 2020, the number of returnees looking for jobs in China has increased significantly, and the number of fresh international students returning to China for jobs has increased.	yes
与2021年相比，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高。	Compared with 2021, the number of fresh international students in 2022 increased by 8.6% year-on-year, and the number of international students returning to China for job search hit a new high.	yes
从回国求职留学生的留学国家分布来看，英国占比最高，为41.4%，其次是澳大利亚(20.3%)和美国(9%)，排名与2021年一致。	Judging from the distribution of study abroad countries for international students returning to China for job search, the United Kingdom accounts for the highest proportion, at 41.4%, followed by Australia (20.3%) and the United States (9%), the ranking is consistent with 2021.	yes
从同比增速来看，2022年来自马来西亚、日本、新加坡的应届留学生人数同比大幅上升，增速分别为66.1%、50.9%和37.7%。	Judging from the year-on-year growth rate, the number of fresh international students from Malaysia, Japan and Singapore has increased significantly year-on-year in 2022, with growth rates of 66.1%, 50.9% and 37.7%, respectively.	yes
来自加拿大、德国、美国、澳大利亚的应届留学生人数同比下降。	The number of fresh international students from Canada, Germany, the United States, and Australia fell year-on-year.	yes
2023春节后第一周海归人才供需走势 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	Chart of the supply and demand of returnee talents in the first week after the Spring Festival in 2023 Source: "2022 China Returnee Employment Survey Report"	yes

河南省规范整合口腔种植医疗服务价格-中新网	Henan Province regulates and integrates the price of oral implant medical services- <url>	yes
央视网消息：种植牙是很多缺牙患者的理想选择，但一直以来，动辄上万元一颗的价格让很多患者望而却步。	CCTV news: Dental implants are an ideal choice for many patients with missing teeth, but the price of tens of thousands of yuan a piece has always discouraged many patients.	yes
今年以来，随着种植牙集采的加速落地，各地也将种植牙降价提上日程。	Since this year, with the acceleration of the collection of dental implants, various places have also put the price reduction of dental implants on the agenda.	yes
从2月10日起，河南省单颗常规种植牙医疗服务价格全流程调控目标为4300元，单颗常规种植全流程费用不高于调控目标的97%。	Starting from February 10, the price of a single conventional implant dental treatment service in Henan Province will be regulated at 4,300 yuan for the whole process, and the cost of a single conventional implant for the whole process will not be higher than 97% of the regulatory target.	yes
种植牙齿指的是一种以植入骨组织内的下部结构为基础来支持、固位上部牙修复体的缺牙修复方式。	Dental implants refer to a method of repairing missing teeth based on the lower structure implanted in the bone tissue to support and retain the upper tooth prosthesis.	yes
记者从郑州大学第一附属医院了解到，以单颗常规种植为例，从种植到最后修复，价格大概要一万六七千元左右。	The reporter learned from the First Affiliated Hospital of Zhengzhou University that taking a single conventional planting as an example, the price from planting to final repair is about 16,000 to 7,000 yuan.	yes
患者 何莹：新政策之后，大夫跟我说，像我这种情况差不多就是8000多元、不到1万元，基本上能省一半。	Patient He Ying: After the new policy, the doctor told me that in a situation like mine, it is almost 8,000 yuan, less than 10,000 yuan, which can basically save half.	yes
在现行项目基础上，河南省还整合确定了“种植体植入费(单颗)”等15个口腔种植类医疗服务价格项目，并统一制定省管公立医疗机构价格和医保支付类别，取消或调整了牙种植体植入术等20个医疗服务价格项目。	On the basis of the current project, Henan Province has also integrated and determined 15 oral implant medical service price items such as “implant implantation fee (single piece)”, and unified the prices of provincial-administered public medical institutions and medical insurance payment categories, cancelled or adjusted 20 medical service price items such as dental implant implantation.	yes
郑州市医疗保障局医药价格和招标采购处处长 李云杰：受益的主要是四方，一个是医保，医保的支出少了；医院的占压少了，病人会适当增加；对供应商来说得到了一个市场；对我们患者来说是得利最大的一方，植一颗牙的费用可能要减半甚至更多。	Li Yunjie, director of the Pharmaceutical Price and Bidding and Procurement Department of Zhengzhou Municipal Medical Security Bureau: The main beneficiaries are four parties. One is medical insurance. The expenditure on medical insurance is less; the hospital's share is less, and the patient will increase appropriately; for suppliers, a market has been obtained; for our patients, it is the most profitable party, and the cost of planting a tooth may have to be halved or even more.	yes

其中提出，2023年底前，建成高速率、大容量、低时延的超级宽带网络，实现“双千兆、全光网、1毫秒、万物联”网络建设目标，打造国内第一、世界领先的极速先锋城市。	It is proposed that a high-speed, large-capacity and low-latency super broadband network will be built before the end of 2023, to achieve the goal of “dual gigabit, all-optical network, 1 millisecond, and everything connected” network construction, and to create the first in China and the world's leading ultra-fast pioneer city.	yes
