2023年底前，10G PON端口占比达到100%，全光工业园区(产业园区)数量超过100家。	By the end of 2023, the proportion of 10G PON ports will reach 100%, and the number of all-optical industrial parks (industrial parks) will exceed 100.	yes
《计划》要求，全面提升5G网络能效。	The "Plan" requires that the energy efficiency of 5G networks be comprehensively improved.	yes
研究制定深圳5G网络服务质量规范标准，开展5G网络测试评估，提升5G网络服务质量。	Research and formulate Shenzhen 5G network service quality specifications and standards, carry out 5G network testing and evaluation, and improve 5G network service quality.	yes
支持基础电信企业加大对重点区域、场所5G网络的优化力度，全年新增5G基站10000个，全市平均下载速率达到500Mbps、上行速率达到100Mbps，重点区域下载速率达到1000Mbps、上行速率达到200Mbps，网络速率和用户体验感大幅提升。	Support basic telecommunications companies to increase the optimization of 5G networks in key areas and places, and 10,000 new 5G base stations will be added throughout the year. The city's average download rate has reached 500Mbps and the uplink rate has reached 100Mbps. The download rate in key areas has reached 1000Mbps and the uplink rate has reached 200Mbps, and the network rate and user experience have been greatly improved.	yes
打造城市级高品质无线局域网。	Create a city-level high-quality wireless local area network.	yes
制定公共场所无线局域网(WLAN)服务规范，推动全市各区人员密集和信息消费需求集中区域WLAN升级，提供千兆接入能力。	Formulate wireless local area network (WLAN) service specifications for public places, promote the upgrading of WLAN in areas with dense personnel and concentrated information consumption needs in various districts of the city, and provide Gigabit access capabilities.	yes
依托“深i网”建设全市公共无线局域网统一认证监管平台，实现“一次认证、无感漫游、智能切换”，支持运营主体将具有公共服务能力的社会自建AP(无线接入点)纳入认证监管平台。	Relying on the "Deep i Network“ to build a unified certification and supervision platform for the city's public wireless local area networks, to achieve ”one-time authentication, sensorless roaming, and intelligent switching", and support operators to incorporate social self-built APS (wireless access points) with public service capabilities into the certification and supervision platform.	no
2023年底前，升级接入AP总量不少于2万个。	Before the end of 2023, the total number of upgraded access APS will not be less than 20,000.	no
此外，《计划》还提出，建设高品质全光运力网络、构建多层次算力供给体系、加快关键通信网络设施建设、提升互联网应用服务能力。	In addition, the "Plan" also proposes to build a high-quality all-optical capacity network, build a multi-level computing power supply system, accelerate the construction of key communication network facilities, and enhance Internet application service capabilities.	no
《计划》明确，协同构建物联感知体系。	The "Plan" is clear and cooperatively builds an IOT perception system.	no
探索以“开源鸿蒙”操作系统为基础，构建城市感知终端建设管理模式，降低对接成本，加快建设城市级物联感知平台，推动市区物联网平台、各领域专业物联网平台网络与数据互联互通。	Explore the construction of an urban perception terminal construction management model based on the ”Open source Hongmeng" operating system, reduce docking costs, accelerate the construction of an urban-level IOT perception platform, and promote the interconnection of urban IOT platforms, professional IOT platforms in various fields, and data.	no
深化物联感知在城市管理、民生服务、公共安全、交通出行等领域应用，拓展城市道路、建筑、公共设施等固定感知与智能网联汽车等移动感知采集渠道。	Deepen the application of IOT perception in urban management, people's livelihood services, public safety, transportation and other fields, and expand fixed perception such as urban roads, buildings, and public facilities, and mobile perception collection channels such as intelligent connected vehicles.	no
2023年底前，水电气物联网感知终端数量超过900万，打造20个多功能智能杆应用示范项目。	By the end of 2023, the number of sensing terminals for the Internet of Things in water and electricity will exceed 9 million, and 20 demonstration projects for the application of multi-function smart poles will be created.	no
《计划》还提到，加强卫星与地面通信融合应用、布局低空网络基础设施建设、推进海上5G网络深度覆盖。	The Plan also mentions strengthening the integration and application of satellite and ground communications, laying out the construction of low-altitude network infrastructure, and promoting the deep coverage of offshore 5G networks.	no

中新网2月11日电 题：中国电商行业涌现“新变量”，带货如何做到“内容为王”？	<url>, February 11th Topic: “New variables” have emerged in China's e-commerce industry. How can the delivery of goods be “content is king”?	yes
中新财经记者 夏宾	China-Singapore Financial Reporter Xia Bin	yes
“我们入局电商算是晚的，但从最开始就意识到，想要从千千万万的店铺中脱颖而出，内容很重要。	“We entered the e-commerce market late, but we realized from the beginning that content is very important to stand out from the millions of stores.	yes
”来自广东的“90后”女生芳芳，现在在抖音电商运营一家滋补食材店铺，让一家有着30多年历史的线下店在线上“开花”。	”Fangfang, a "post-90s" girl from Guangdong, now operates a nourishing food store on Douyin e-commerce, allowing an offline store with a history of more than 30 years to “blossom” online.	yes
模仿老港片影调、配上经典粤语歌，打开@芳芳一人食抖音账号，精美的视频令人耳目一新。	Imitating the tone of old Hong Kong movies and accompanied by classic Cantonese songs, open the @Fangfang one-person food Douyin account. The exquisite videos are refreshing.	yes
在近日举行的抖音电商“寻找同行者·优质内容分享专场”上，芳芳作为优质创作者代表到场发言，介绍了日常创作的经历和体会。	At the recently held Douyin e-commerce “Looking for Peers· High-quality Content sharing Session”, Fangfang spoke as a representative of high-quality creators and introduced her daily creative experience and experience.	yes
她在现场说：“精心打磨的视频收获了很多网友的关注，好多人对我家的食材感兴趣，想跟着一起做美食，销路就一下子打开了。	She said at the scene: “The carefully polished video has gained the attention of many netizens. Many people are interested in the ingredients of my family and want to cook food together, so the sales market suddenly opened.	yes
”	”	yes
芳芳靠着煲汤视频让更多人爱上“老广的味道”，一场直播最多卖出30万件滋补食材，挽救了家里濒临倒闭的老店。	Fangfang relied on the soup-making video to make more people fall in love with the ”taste of Laoguang". A live broadcast sold up to 300,000 pieces of nourishing ingredients, saving her family's old shop that was on the verge of collapse.	no
“无内容，不电商”，随着短视频和直播电商不断发展，人们对电商内容的要求和标准正步入新阶段。	“No content, no e-commerce”, with the continuous development of short videos and live e-commerce, people's requirements and standards for e-commerce content are entering a new stage.	no
直播带货发展初期，直播间往往用低价折扣吸引用户，价格优势似乎成了当时的唯一卖点。	In the early days of the development of live broadcast with goods, live broadcast studios often used low-cost discounts to attract users, and price advantages seemed to be the only selling point at that time.	no
近年来，既有刘畊宏、东方甄选等现象级大V，也有在垂直细分领域出现的不少非大众所知的达人和商家，他们通过持续打造符合自己品牌调性的优质内容，提升长期经营效益。	In recent years, there have been both phenomenon-level big V's such as Liu Yuhong and Dongfang Selection, as well as many people and businesses that are not well-known to the public in vertical segments. 抖音电商明星作者运营负责人高亚轩介绍，过去一年有627万创作者通过抖音电商将内容变现，他们的内容创作量增长了252%，总成交额也翻了一倍以上。	Gao Yaxuan, head of star author operations for Douyin e-commerce, introduced that in the past year, 6.27 million creators have monetized content through Douyin e-commerce, and their content creation volume has increased by 252%, and the total turnover has more than doubled.	no
“在这些数字背后，我们能感受到一个蓬勃生长、具有旺盛生命力的作者生态。	“Behind these numbers, we can feel a vigorous and vigorous author ecology.	no
”高亚轩说。	"Gao Yaxuan said.	no
北京师范大学传播创新与未来媒体实验平台此前发布了《电商行业内容生态健康指数(ECHI)报告》，从数据维度解析了当前电商行业中“新变量”——优质内容的重要性，运用指数对国内27家主流电商平台内容生态情况进行了评估。	The Communication Innovation and Future Media Experimental Platform of Beijing Normal University previously released the “E-commerce Industry Content Ecological Health Index (ECHI) Report”, which analyzes the importance of high-quality content, a "new variable" in the current e-commerce industry, from the data dimension, and uses the index to evaluate the content ecology of 27 mainstream e-commerce platforms in China. The ecological situation was evaluated.	no
根据上述报告的电商行业内容生态健康指数排名，抖音电商、快手、淘宝、拼多多、京东位居前五。	According to the ranking of the ecological health index of the content of the e-commerce industry in the above report, Douyin e-commerce, Kuaishou, Taobao, Pinduoduo, and Jingdong ranked in the top five.	no
报告认为，电商行业内容生态是一个综合性概念，是将电商与内容进行整合，但并非所有内容都可与电商整合，好的PGC(专业生产内容)与UGC(用户原创内容)才是与电商进行整合的优质载体，内容平台价值越高，消费与推广的场景也就越来越丰富，电商植入的可能性也就越高，商业价值也就越强，这种公共领域和私人领域逐步集成分布的电商内容生产和内容消费的比例也就会越高。	The report believes that the content ecology of the e-commerce industry is a comprehensive concept that integrates e-commerce with content, but not all content can be integrated with e-commerce. Good PGC (professional production of content) and UGC (user original content) are the high-quality carriers for integration with e-commerce. The higher the value of the content platform, the richer the consumption and promotion scenarios, the higher the possibility of e-commerce implantation, and the stronger the commercial value, the higher the proportion of e-commerce content production and content consumption that are gradually integrated and distributed in the public and private sectors.	no
现场，北京师范大学新闻传播学院教授、中国传媒经济与管理专业委员会理事长喻国明对《报告》做了分析解读。	At the scene, Yu Guoming, a professor of the School of Journalism and Communication of Beijing Normal University and chairman of the China Media Economics and Management Professional Committee, analyzed and interpreted the report.	no
他表示，就内容价值而言，当前电商行业已经从“消费可及性”过渡到“消费品质化”阶段，优质、专业、差异化的内容是电商行业的“硬通货”。	He said that in terms of content value, the current e-commerce industry has transitioned from “consumer accessibility” to “consumer quality” stage, and high-quality, professional and differentiated content is the “hard currency” of the e-commerce industry.	no
同时，内容成为电商发展新阶段的根本和抓手，知识付费、专业性知识、KOL(关键意见领袖)等PGC内容开始在电商直播中成为标配。	At the same time, content has become the foundation and gripper of the new stage of e-commerce development, and PGC content such as knowledge payment, professional knowledge, and KOL (key opinion leaders) have begun to become standard in e-commerce live broadcasts.	no
展望电商行业的未来发展，喻国明提出两方面的建议。	Looking forward to the future development of the e-commerce industry, Yu Guoming put forward two suggestions.	no
一个是从内容结构提升的角度看，推动电商内容生态健康程度和质量整体提升，打造正向内容创作和管理标准，实现电商行业内容生态健康系统指数与动态均衡。	One is to promote the overall improvement of the ecological health and quality of e-commerce content from the perspective of content structure improvement, create positive content creation and management standards, and realize the index and dynamic balance of the content ecological health system of the e-commerce industry.	no
另一个是从外部生态看，要实现内容电商行业的健康发展和外部环境的价值协同与共创。	The other is from the perspective of external ecology, to achieve the healthy development of the content e-commerce industry and the value synergy and co-creation of the external environment.	no
“未来电商行业还需要更多的数据、人工智能方面的支持，形成对未来发展稳定性的预测；此外，为商家提供更规范、健康的成长空间，实现电商行业中企业、用户、产品与服务的价值协同，共创健康内容生态。	“In the future, the e-commerce industry will need more data and artificial intelligence support to form a forecast of the stability of future development; in addition, it will provide businesses with a more standardized and healthy growth space, realize the value synergy of enterprises, users, products and services in the e-commerce industry, and create a healthy content ecosystem.	no
”(完)	”(End)	no
北交所融资融券交易业务下周启动-中新网	The margin trading business of the Beijing Stock Exchange will start next week- <url>	yes
本报讯(记者 孙杰)昨晚，北交所发布消息，经中国证监会批准，北京证券交易所融资融券交易业务将于2月13日正式启动，届时已取得北交所融资融券交易权限的证券公司可接受投资者委托，向北交所进行融资融券交易申报。	Newspaper news (reporter Sun Jie) Last night, the Beijing Stock Exchange released news that with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, the margin trading business of the Beijing Stock Exchange will be officially launched on February 13. At that time, securities companies that have obtained the margin trading authority of the Beijing Stock Exchange can accept investors' commissions and declare margin trading to the Beijing Stock Exchange.	yes
首批56只融资融券标的股票名单以2023年1月31日为计算基准日确定。	The list of the first batch of 56 underlying stocks for margin financing is determined on January 31, 2023 as the calculation base date.	yes
北交所表示，融资融券标的股票名单和可充抵保证金证券名单将通过北交所官网的“信息披露-融资融券信息”栏目公布，方便投资者查询。	The Beijing Stock Exchange said that the list of stocks subject to margin financing and the list of margin-deductible securities will be announced through the “Information Disclosure-Margin financing Information” section of the official website of the Beijing Stock Exchange to facilitate investors' inquiries.	yes
融资融券是证券市场重要的基础性制度，也是国际证券市场中较为成熟的交易方式。	Margin financing is an important basic system in the securities market and a more mature trading method in the international securities market.	yes
去年9月2日，在宣布设立一周年之际，北交所对融资融券业务公开征求意见。	On September 2 last year, on the occasion of the first anniversary of the announcement of its establishment, the Beijing Stock Exchange publicly solicited opinions on the margin business.	yes
北交所融资融券交易的启动是持续推进北交所市场制度建设、完善交易机制、提升二级市场定价功能的重要举措。	The launch of margin trading on the Beijing Stock Exchange is an important measure to continuously promote the construction of the market system of the Beijing Stock Exchange, improve the trading mechanism, and enhance the pricing function of the secondary market.	yes
融资融券制度有利于丰富投资者交易策略，满足投资者多元交易需求，促进市场价格发现，进一步提升市场流动性。	The margin system is conducive to enriching investors' trading strategies, meeting investors' diversified trading needs, promoting market price discovery, and further enhancing market liquidity.	yes
下一步，北交所将在中国证监会的领导下，持续做好融资融券业务各项保障工作，以投资者需求为导向丰富交易制度工具，完善相关配套机制，着力打造服务创新型中小企业的一流交易所。	In the next step, the Beijing Stock Exchange, under the leadership of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, will continue to do a good job in guaranteeing the financing and margin business, enrich the trading system tools based on investor needs, improve relevant supporting mechanisms, and strive to build a first-class exchange serving innovative small and medium-sized enterprises.	yes

“推进中国式现代化是一个系统工程，需要统筹兼顾、系统谋划、整体推进，正确处理好顶层设计与实践探索、战略与策略、守正与创新、效率与公平、活力与秩序、自立自强与对外开放等一系列重大关系。	“Promoting Chinese-style modernization is a systematic project that requires comprehensive consideration, systematic planning, and overall promotion, and correctly handles a series of major relationships such as top-level design and practical exploration, strategy and strategy, integrity and innovation, efficiency and fairness, vitality and order, self-reliance and opening up to the outside world.	yes
”在新进中央委员会的委员、候补委员和省部级主要领导干部学习贯彻习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想和党的二十大精神研讨班开班式上，习近平总书记科学把握现代化建设规律，深入系统阐明实践中需要处理好的一系列重大关系，为我们大力推进中国式现代化提供了科学方法论。	”At the opening ceremony of the seminar for new members of the Central Committee, alternate members and major leading cadres at the provincial and ministerial levels to learn and implement Xi Jinping's new era of socialism with Chinese characteristics and the spirit of the Party's 20th National Congress, General Secretary Xi Jinping scientifically grasped the laws of modernization and systematically clarified a series of major relationships that need to be dealt with in practice, which provides a scientific methodology for us to vigorously promote Chinese-style modernization.	yes
推进中国式现代化涉及经济、政治、文化、社会、生态文明等各个领域，关系治党治国治军、内政外交国防等方方面面，既要做好系统谋划，又要勇于改革创新，不断实现整体推进。	Promoting Chinese-style modernization involves various fields such as economy, politics, culture, society, and ecological civilization. It is related to the governance of the party, the country, the army, internal affairs, diplomacy, and national defense. It is necessary not only to make systematic plans, but also to have the courage to reform and innovate, and continuously achieve overall advancement.	yes
进行顶层设计，需要深刻洞察世界发展大势，准确把握人民群众的共同愿望，深入探索经济社会发展规律，使制定的规划和政策体系体现时代性、把握规律性、富于创造性，做到远近结合、上下贯通、内容协调。	To carry out top-level design, it is necessary to have a deep insight into the general development trend of the world, accurately grasp the common aspirations of the people, and deeply explore the laws of economic and social development, so that the formulated planning and policy system reflects the times, grasps regularity, and is full of creativity, so as to achieve a combination of distance and near, top-to-bottom connection, and content coordination.	yes
推进中国式现代化是一个探索性事业，还有许多未知领域，需要在实践中去大胆探索，通过改革创新来推动事业发展，决不能刻舟求剑、守株待兔。	Promoting Chinese-style modernization is an exploratory undertaking. There are still many uncharted areas that need to be boldly explored in practice and promoted through reform and innovation. We must not seek swords and wait for the hare.	yes
战略问题是一个政党、一个国家的根本性问题。	Strategic issues are fundamental issues for a political party and a country.	yes
推进中国式现代化，要增强战略的前瞻性，以科学的战略预见未来、引领未来；要增强战略的全局性，着眼于解决事关党和国家事业兴衰成败、牵一发而动全身的重大问题；要增强战略的稳定性，战略一经形成，就要长期坚持、一抓到底、善作善成。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, it is necessary to enhance the forward-looking strategy, foresee the future and lead the future with a scientific strategy; to enhance the global nature of the strategy, focusing on solving major issues related to the rise and fall of the party and the national cause, which affect the whole body; to enhance the stability of the strategy, once the strategy is formed, it is necessary to persevere for a long time, grasp it to the end, and do good deeds.	yes
要科学把握战略和策略的辩证统一关系，把战略的原则性和策略的灵活性有机结合起来，灵活机动、随机应变、临机决断，在因地制宜、因势而动、顺势而为中把握战略主动。	It is necessary to scientifically grasp the dialectical unified relationship between strategy and strategy, organically combine the principle of strategy with the flexibility of strategy, be flexible, adaptable, and make decisions on the spot, and grasp the strategic initiative in adapting to local conditions, moving according to the situation, and taking advantage of the situation.	no
中华民族是守正创新的民族。	The Chinese nation is a nation of integrity and innovation.	no
处理好守正与创新的关系，既要守好中国式现代化的本和源、根和魂，毫不动摇坚持中国式现代化的中国特色、本质要求、重大原则，确保中国式现代化的正确方向，又要把创新摆在国家发展全局的突出位置，顺应时代发展要求，着眼于解决重大理论和实践问题，积极识变应变求变，大力推进改革创新，不断塑造发展新动能新优势，充分激发全社会创造活力。	To deal with the relationship between integrity and innovation, we must not only abide by the origin and source, root and soul of Chinese-style modernization, and unswervingly adhere to the Chinese characteristics, essential requirements, and major principles of Chinese-style modernization to ensure the correct direction of Chinese-style modernization, but also put innovation in a prominent position in the overall development of the country, conform to the development requirements of the times, focus on solving major theoretical and practical problems, actively recognize changes and adapt to changes, vigorously promote reform and innovation, and constantly shape new kinetic energy and advantages for development, so as to fully stimulate the vitality of the whole society.	no
效率是公平的重要基础，公平是效率的有力保证。	Efficiency is an important foundation of fairness, and fairness is a strong guarantee of efficiency.	no
我们推进中国式现代化，既要创造比资本主义更高的效率，又要更有效地维护社会公平，更好实现效率与公平相兼顾、相促进、相统一。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, we must not only create higher efficiency than capitalism, but also more effectively maintain social fairness, and better realize the balance, promotion, and unification of efficiency and fairness.	no
处理好效率与公平的关系，不断实现发展为了人民、发展依靠人民、发展成果由人民共享，让现代化建设成果更多更公平惠及全体人民。	Handle the relationship between efficiency and fairness well, and continuously realize that development is for the people, development depends on the people, and the results of development are shared by the people, so that the results of modernization can benefit all the people more and more fairly.	no
推进中国式现代化，需要处理好活力与秩序的关系，让社会既充满活力又安定有序。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, it is necessary to deal with the relationship between vitality and order so that society can be both vibrant and stable and orderly.	no
要统筹好发展和安全两件大事，贯彻总体国家安全观，健全国家安全体系，增强维护国家安全能力，坚定维护国家政权安全、制度安全、意识形态安全和重点领域安全。	It is necessary to co-ordinate the two major events of development and security, implement the overall concept of national security, improve the national security system, strengthen the ability to maintain national security, and firmly maintain the security of national power, institutional security, ideological security, and key areas.	no
既在发展中更多考虑安全因素，通过发展提升国家安全实力，运用发展成果来夯实国家安全的基础，又善于营造有利于经济社会发展的安全环境，不断激发发展活力，实现高质量发展和高水平安全的良性互动。	Not only do we pay more attention to security factors in development, enhance national security strength through development, and use development results to consolidate the foundation of national security, but we are also good at creating a security environment conducive to economic and social development, continuously stimulating development vitality, and achieving healthy interaction between high-quality development and high-level security.	no
推进中国式现代化，既要坚持走自己的路，又要拓展世界眼光，坚持对外开放，不断拓展中国式现代化的广度和深度。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, we must not only adhere to our own path, but also expand the vision of the world, adhere to opening up to the outside world, and constantly expand the breadth and depth of Chinese-style modernization.	no
要坚持独立自主、自立自强，坚持把国家和民族发展放在自己力量的基点上，坚持把我国发展进步的命运牢牢掌握在自己手中。	We must adhere to independence, self-reliance and self-improvement, insist on putting the development of the country and the nation on the basis of our own strength, and insist on firmly holding the fate of our country's development and progress in our own hands.	no
要不断扩大高水平对外开放，深度参与全球产业分工和合作，用好国内国际两种资源，拓展中国式现代化的发展空间，在互利共赢中共享发展机遇、共创美好未来。	We must continue to expand high-level opening up to the outside world, deeply participate in the global industrial division of labor and cooperation, make good use of domestic and international resources, expand the development space of Chinese-style modernization, and share development opportunities and create a better future in mutual benefit and win-win situation.	no
循道而行，方能致远。	Only by following the way can we go far.	no
让我们在以习近平同志为核心的党中央坚强领导下、在习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想科学指引下，把握规律、笃行不怠，充分发挥积极性、主动性、创造性，正确处理好一系列重大关系，在全面建设社会主义现代化国家新征程上奋发有为，不断开辟中国式现代化新境界。	Let us, under the strong leadership of the Party Central Committee with Comrade Xi Jinping as the core, and under the scientific guidance of Xi Jinping's socialist thought with Chinese characteristics in the new era, grasp the rules, practice without slackening, give full play to enthusiasm, initiative, and creativity, properly handle a series of major relationships, and work hard on the new journey of building a modern socialist country in an all-round way, and constantly open up a new realm of Chinese-style modernization.	no
（德国之声中文网）拜登政府本周五（2月10日）将6个与疑似参与间谍气球计划的中国实体列入黑名单。	(Deutsche Welle Chinese website) The Biden administration on Friday (February 10) blacklisted six Chinese entities suspected of participating in the spy balloon program.	yes
美国商务部表示，这5家中国公司及1家研究机构帮助中国军队现代化，尤其是航空航天项目，包括飞艇和飞机。	The U.S. Department of Commerce said that these five Chinese companies and one research institute have helped modernize the Chinese military, especially aerospace projects, including airships and aircraft.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司很难获得美国的技术出口。	It is difficult for blacklisted companies to obtain U.S. technology exports.	yes
名单被称为“实体名单”（entity list），入列的公司除非获得美国商务部的特别出口许可证，否则将无法向美国供应商购买技术或商品。	The list is called the ”entity list" (entity list). Unless the listed companies obtain a special export license from the U.S. Department of Commerce, they will not be able to purchase technology or goods from U.S. suppliers.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司是：北京南江空天科技股份有限公司、中国电子科技集团第四十八研究所、东莞凌空遥感科技有限公司、鹰门航空科技集团有限公司、广州天海翔航空科技有限公司和山西鹰门航空科技集团有限公司。	The blacklisted companies are: Beijing Nanjiang Aerospace Technology Co., Ltd., the 48th Research Institute of China Electronic Technology Group, Dongguan Lingkong Remote Sensing Technology Co., Ltd., Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd., Guangzhou Tianhaixiang Aviation Technology Co., Ltd. and Shanxi Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd.	yes
在此之前，白宫表示考虑做出更广泛措施，“揭露和处理”中国威胁美国国家安全的更大规模监控活动。	Prior to this, the White House said it was considering broader measures to “expose and deal with” China's larger surveillance activities that threaten U.S. national security.	yes
气球事件引发中美之间进一步紧张，美国国务卿布林肯取消了访问中国的行程。	The balloon incident triggered further tensions between China and the United States, and U.S. Secretary of State Blinken cancelled his visit to China.	yes
美国2月4日击落气球，中国政府向美国驻华使馆提出严正交涉，批评美国严重冲击和损害双方稳定中美关系的努力和进程。	The United States shot down the balloon on February 4, and the Chinese government submitted serious negotiations to the U.S. Embassy in China, criticizing the U.S. for seriously impacting and harming the efforts and processes of the two sides to stabilize Sino-U.S. relations.	yes
从现有残骸证据及中国军方的采购平台资讯，美国政府得出结论，认为该气球的制造厂商“跟中国解放军有直接关系”，而且是中国军方批准的供应商。	From the existing wreckage evidence and information from the Chinese military's procurement platform, the U.S. government concluded that the manufacturer of the balloon “has a direct relationship with the Chinese People's Liberation Army” and is an approved supplier by the Chinese military.	yes
中国外交部发言人毛宁在周五的新闻发布会上表示，关于一只中国无人民用飞艇因不可抗力误入美国领空的意外事件，中方已经多次说明情况、阐明立场。	Mao Ning, a spokesperson for the Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, said at a press conference on Friday that China has repeatedly explained the situation and clarified its position regarding the accidental incident of a Chinese unmanned civilian airship straying into U.S. airspace due to force majeure.	yes
根据外交部网站，她补充表示，美国国会的有关决议案纯属政治操弄和炒作。	According to the website of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, she added that the relevant resolutions of the United States Congress are purely political manipulation and speculation.	no
中方对此强烈不满、坚决反对。	China is strongly dissatisfied with this and resolutely opposes it.	no
美国商务部负责出口执法的助理部长阿克塞尔罗德(Matthew Axelrod)表示： “今天的行动表明，我们查明并阻止中国使用间谍气球而做出的共同努力，这些气球侵犯了美国和40多个国家的领空。	Matthew Axelrod, assistant secretary for export enforcement at the U.S. Department of Commerce, said: “Today's actions demonstrate our joint efforts to identify and prevent China from using spy balloons that violate the airspace of the United States and more than 40 countries.	no
”	”	no
路透社报道，广州天海翔航空科技有限公司的一名员工表示对制裁并不知情，并拒绝进一步评论。	Reuters reported that an employee of Guangzhou Tianhaixiang Aviation Technology Co., Ltd. said he was not aware of the sanctions and declined to comment further.	no
中国驻美国大使馆和尚未对这些信息发表评论。	The Chinese Embassy in the United States has not yet commented on this information.	no

（德国之声中文网）距离土耳其和叙利亚部分地区发生地震已经过去数日，找到幸存者的希望日渐渺茫，然而在周六获救的一家五口却令搜救人员感到无比欣慰。	(German Voice Chinese network) It has been a few days since the earthquake in parts of Turkey and Syria, and the hope of finding survivors is getting slimmer. However, the family of five rescued on Saturday made the search and rescue personnel feel extremely relieved.	yes
据美联社报道，在加济安泰普省的重灾区努尔达伊镇，这个五口之家在废墟之下受困五天多之后，被成功营救。	According to the Associated Press, in the town of Nurdayy, the hardest-hit area in Gaziantep Province, the family of five was successfully rescued after being trapped under the ruins for more than five days.	yes
搜救人员先是从一堆废墟中拉出了母亲和女儿，随后找到了父亲，但他坚持要求先救自己的儿子和另一个女儿。	The search and rescue personnel first pulled out the mother and daughter from a pile of ruins, and then found the father, but he insisted on saving his son and another daughter first.	yes
当他们全部获救之后，人群中响起了欢呼声。	When they were all rescued, cheers rang out in the crowd.	yes
在土耳其南部城市卡赫拉曼马拉什，在恶劣的严寒天气条件下，一个16岁的少年和一位70岁老妪也被成功营救。	In the southern Turkish city of Kahramanmarash, a 16-year-old boy and a 70-year-old woman were also successfully rescued under severe cold weather conditions.	yes
“今天是什么日子了？	“What day is it today?	yes
”——这个被困废墟之下129小时的少年在被带回到地面上之后问营救自己的搜救员。	”--The teenager who was trapped under the ruins for 129 hours asked the rescuers who rescued him after being brought back to the ground.	yes
一位卡赫拉曼马拉什的男子抱着他刚刚获救的猫	A man from Kahramanmarash is holding his newly rescued cat	yes
奇迹般的成功营救案例给原本已经希望渺茫的搜救工作带来了一线曙光，然而与此同时，遇难人数也在不断上升。	The miraculous successful rescue cases have brought a glimmer of light to the search and rescue work that had been promising, but at the same time, the number of people killed is also rising.	yes
目前根据官方统计，周一的地震已经在土耳其造成超过2万人死亡，邻国叙利亚的死亡人数估计在3500人以上。	According to official statistics, Monday's earthquake has killed more than 20,000 people in Turkey, and the death toll in neighboring Syria is estimated to be more than 3,500.	yes
尽管专家表示，人在被困废墟之后最多还能存活一周以上的时间，但是寻找到更多幸存者的希望已经变得愈加渺茫。	Although experts say that people can survive for more than a week at most after being trapped in the ruins, the hope of finding more survivors has become increasingly slim.	no
救援人员仍然在借助热成像仪来探寻废墟之下的生命迹象。	Rescuers are still using thermal imagers to explore signs of life under the ruins.	no
与此同时，救援工作的重点开始转向帮助那些急需救助的幸存者。	At the same time, the focus of rescue efforts began to shift to helping survivors who were in urgent need of assistance.	no
联合国官员：该地区“百年未遇”的灾难	UN official: A disaster “not encountered in a hundred years” in the region	no
主管人道主义事务的联合国副秘书长兼紧急救济协调员马丁·格里菲思（Martin Griffiths）在土耳其召开的记者会上表示，这次地震是该地区“百年以来最糟糕的一次灾难”。	Martin Griffith, the United Nations Under-Secretary-General for Humanitarian Affairs and Emergency Relief Coordinator, said at a press conference in Turkey that the earthquake was “the worst disaster in a hundred years” in the region.	no
他还称赞土耳其在灾后的应对行动是“非同寻常”的。	He also praised Turkey's response after the disaster as “extraordinary.”	no

联合国承诺向叙利亚的地震灾区民众额外提供2500万美元的救援捐款。	The United Nations has promised to provide an additional US225 million in relief donations to the people in the earthquake-stricken areas of Syria.	no

60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
智利大地震（1960年）	The Great Chilean Earthquake (1960)	no
当地时间1960年5月22日下午3点11分，智利瓦尔迪维亚发生人类史上观测记录到的规模最大的地震，地震矩规模为9.5。	At 3:11 pm local time on May 22, 1960, the largest earthquake observed and recorded in human history occurred in Valdivia, Chile, with a moment magnitude of 9.5.	no
短短十分钟内，瓦尔迪维亚整座城市变为废墟。	In just ten minutes, the entire city of Valdivia turned into ruins.	no
地震之后引发的巨大海啸袭击到智利海岸线，掀起浪高高度是25米高的巨大海啸。	The huge tsunami caused by the earthquake hit the Chilean coastline, setting off a huge tsunami with a wave height of 25 meters high.	no
海啸波及到遥远的日本、菲律宾。	The tsunami spread to distant Japan and the Philippines.	no
如此范围的灾难所造成的罹难人数以及经济损失无法精确得知。	The number of victims and economic losses caused by a disaster of this magnitude cannot be accurately known.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
阿拉斯加大地震（1964年）	Great Alaska Earthquake (1964)	no
1964年3月27日是一个星期五，也是是耶稣受难日。	March 27, 1964 was a Friday, and it was also Good Friday.	no
这一天美国阿拉斯加发生北美洲历史上最大的地震，矩震级达到9.2。	On this day, the largest earthquake in North American history occurred in Alaska, with a moment magnitude of 9.2.	no
直到2006年，阿拉斯加大地震仍然是有纪录以来世界第三大地震。	Until 2006, the Great Alaska Earthquake was still the third largest earthquake in the world on record.	no
地震发生时，太平洋板块和北美洲板块之间的一个断层在威廉王子湾接近学院峡湾的地方断裂。	At the time of the earthquake, a fault between the Pacific Plate and the North American Plate broke in Prince William Bay near College Sound.	no
在大部分的地区这场地震持续了3分钟到5分钟。	In most areas, the earthquake lasted from 3 minutes to 5 minutes.	no
海床位移引发了巨大的海啸，高度为67米。	The displacement of the seabed triggered a huge tsunami with a height of 67 meters.	no
由于当天是假日，所以学校和许多企业都关闭了。	Since the day was a holiday, schools and many businesses were closed.	no
这场大地震最后导致了139人罹难。	The earthquake eventually killed 139 people.	no
其中9人直接死于地震，其他130人死于地震引发的海啸。	Among them, 9 people died directly from the earthquake, and the other 130 people died from the tsunami caused by the earthquake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
唐山大地震（1976年）	Tangshan Earthquake (1976)	no
1976年7月28日，中国河北省唐山市和丰南县在16小时内发生两次7级以上强烈地震。	On July 28, 1976, two strong earthquakes of magnitude 7 or higher occurred in Tangshan City and Fengnan County, Hebei Province, China within 16 hours.	no
震源距地面23千米。	The source of the earthquake was 23 kilometers from the ground.	no
唐山市全市交通、通讯、供水、供电中断，顷刻间被夷为平地。	The city's transportation, communications, water supply, and power supply in Tangshan City were interrupted, and it was razed to the ground in an instant.	no
140公里外的首都北京也有强烈震感。	A strong earthquake was also felt in Beijing, the capital 140 kilometers away.	no
据官方统计，包括北京、天津在内的所有受灾地区，地震造成242769人死亡，164851人重伤。	According to official statistics, in all affected areas, including Beijing and Tianjin, the earthquake caused 242,769 deaths and 164,851 serious injuries.	no
唐山大地震成为中国有记录至今第二多人死亡的地震，仅次于1556年嘉靖大地震。	The Tangshan Earthquake became the second deadliest earthquake on record in China, second only to the Great Jiajing Earthquake in 1556.	no
但是有海外科学家估计，这场地震可能造成至少65万人死亡。	But some overseas scientists estimate that the earthquake may have killed at least 650,000 people.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
印度洋大地震（2004年）	The Great Indian Ocean Earthquake (2004)	no
2004年12月26日，印尼苏门答腊岛亚齐省西岸160公里处发生地震，震源深度30公里，矩震级9.1到9.3。	On December 26, 2004, an earthquake occurred 160 kilometers off the west coast of Aceh Province, Sumatra, Indonesia, with a depth of 30 kilometers and a moment magnitude of 9.1 to 9.3.	no
地震引发了浪高高度达15到30米的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a huge tsunami with a wave height of 15 to 30 meters.	no
太平洋沿岸总共14个国家被波及，其中受灾严重最严重的地区包括印尼亚齐省、泰国镐立和普吉岛渡假区、斯里兰卡和印度泰米尔邦。	A total of 14 countries on the Pacific coast were affected, of which the most severely affected areas included Aceh Province in Indonesia, the resort areas of Koh Li and Phuket in Thailand, Sri Lanka and the Indian state of Tamil Nadu.	no
当时正值圣诞节的旅游旺季，受灾地区聚集了大量的旅客和本地居民，导致许多在沙滩上享受假期的旅客和在海边工作的当地人被海啸卷到海底，使这次地震不少人成为失踪者。	At that time, it was the peak tourist season of Christmas. A large number of tourists and local residents gathered in the affected areas, resulting in many tourists enjoying holidays on the beach and locals working by the sea being swept to the bottom of the sea by the tsunami, making many people missing in the earthquake.	no
据估计，罹难人数和失踪人数至少有30万人。	It is estimated that the number of dead and missing is at least 300,000.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
汶川大地震（2008年）	Wenchuan Earthquake (2008)	no
2008年5月12日，中国四川省汶川地区发生大地震。	On May 12, 2008, a major earthquake occurred in Wenchuan, Sichuan Province, China.	no
根据中国地震局的数据，此次地震的面波震级达8.2级、矩震级达8.3级，破坏地区超过10万平方公里。	According to data from the China Earthquake Administration, the earthquake had a surface wave magnitude of 8.2 and a moment magnitude of 8.3, and the damage area exceeded 100,000 square kilometers.	no
截至2008年9月25日，地震共计造成69227人遇难，17923人失踪，374643人不同程度受伤，1993.03万人失去住所，受灾总人口达4625.6万人。	As of September 25, 2008, the earthquake had killed a total of 69,227 people, 17,923 people were missing, 374,643 people were injured to varying degrees, 19.9303 million people lost their homes, and the total affected population reached 46.256 million.	no
是中华人民共和国成立以来破坏力最大的地震，也是唐山大地震后伤亡最惨重的一次。	It was the most destructive earthquake since the founding of the People's Republic of China, and it was also the one with the heaviest casualties after the Tangshan Earthquake.	no
2009年3月，中国国务院宣布将每年的5月12日定为防灾减灾日，加强对民众的教育和对防灾减灾工作的关注。	In March 2009, the State Council of China announced that May 12th of each year will be designated as Disaster prevention and Mitigation Day to strengthen public education and pay attention to disaster prevention and mitigation.	no
之后中国多地政府和中小学在每年这一天举行防震演习。	After that, many governments and primary and secondary schools in China held earthquake-proof exercises on this day of the year.	no
中小学也开始重视普及“防震减灾”教育。	Primary and secondary schools have also begun to pay attention to popularizing “earthquake prevention and disaster reduction” education.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
海地地震（2010年）	Haiti Earthquake (2010)	no
2010年1月12日，加勒比海岛国海地发生里氏7.0级的地震。	On January 12, 2010, an earthquake with a magnitude of 7.0 on the Richter scale occurred in Haiti, an island country in the Caribbean Sea.	no
震中位于海地首都太子港以西南方25公里，震源距离地表13千米左右。	The epicenter of the earthquake was located 25 kilometers west and south of Port-au-Prince, the capital of Haiti, and the source of the earthquake was about 13 kilometers from the surface.	no
国际红十字会估计，受到地震影响的人口大约为300万。	The International Red Cross estimates that the population affected by the earthquake is about 3 million.	no
海地政府公布的确认死亡人数超过20万。	The confirmed death toll announced by the Haitian government exceeded 200,000.	no
海地国内的一些地区，多达90%的房屋在地震中被摧毁。	In some areas of Haiti, as many as 90% of houses were destroyed in the earthquake.	no
虽然国际社会提供了大量援助和支持，但是这个人口过剩腐败横行的贫困国家从未从这场灾难中恢复过来。	Although the international community has provided a lot of assistance and support, this poor country with overpopulation and rampant corruption has never recovered from this disaster.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
日本东北大地震（2011年）	The Great Tohoku Earthquake in Japan (2011)	no
2011年3月11日日本东北地方外海发生矩震级为9.0的大型逆冲区地震。	On March 11, 2011, a large-scale thrust zone earthquake with a moment magnitude of 9.0 occurred off the coast of Northeast Japan.	no
震中位于在宫城县首府仙台市以东的太平洋海域，震源深度测得数据为24千米，并且引发最大爬高40.1米的巨大海啸。	The epicenter of the earthquake was located in the Pacific Ocean east of Sendai City, the capital of Miyagi Prefecture. The depth of the source was measured at 24 kilometers, and it triggered a huge tsunami with a maximum height of 40.1 meters.	no
这场地震是日本有观测纪录到以来第一个震级超过9的地震。	This earthquake was the first earthquake with a magnitude of more than 9 in Japan since it was observed and recorded.	no
约有2.2万人在灾害丧生，大约40万座建筑被完全摧毁或倒塌。	About 22,000 people lost their lives in the disaster, and about 400,000 buildings were completely destroyed or collapsed.	no
福岛第一核电站受地震海啸影响发生泄漏事故。	The Fukushima Daiichi nuclear power plant was affected by the earthquake and tsunami and a leakage accident occurred.	no
这次事故在国际核事件分级表（INES）中被分类为最严重的7级。	The accident was classified as the most serious level 7 in the International Nuclear Incident Classification Table (INES).	no
福岛核事故导致在全世界都测量到微量辐射性物质，包括碘-131、铯-137（半衰期为30年）在内。	The Fukushima nuclear accident caused trace amounts of radioactive substances to be measured all over the world, including iodine-131 and cesium-137 (with a half-life of 30 years).	no
大量放射性同位素因此核事故释入太平洋。	A large number of radioactive isotopes were released into the Pacific Ocean as a result of a nuclear accident.	no
根据联合国的统计，在土叙两国灾区，目前至少有87万人急需食物。	According to statistics from the United Nations, at least 870,000 people in the disaster areas of Turkey and Syria are currently in urgent need of food.	no
仅仅在叙利亚，就有多达530万人因为地震而失去家园。	In Syria alone, as many as 5.3 million people have lost their homes due to the earthquake.	no
世界粮食计划署（WFP）呼吁拨款7700万美元，为土耳其和叙利亚因为地震而流离失所的灾民提供食物。	The World Food Programme (WFP) has called for an allocation of US777 million to provide food to victims displaced by the earthquake in Turkey and Syria.	no
目前灾区气温低至零下，很多灾民没有住所。	At present, the temperature in the disaster area is as low as minus, and many victims have no shelter.	no
土耳其政府分发了大量的热餐、帐篷和毯子，但是这些物资仍然难以送达很多急需帮助的人。	The Turkish government has distributed a large number of hot meals, tents and blankets, but these supplies are still difficult to reach many people in urgent need.	no
而在深陷内战泥潭长达12年之久的叙利亚，地震则使民众的苦难处境雪上加霜。	In Syria, which has been mired in civil war for 12 years, the earthquake has made the suffering of the people even worse.	no
在地震发生后的四天内，世界粮食计划署已经向土耳其和叙利亚的11.5万人提供了食物救济。	In the four days after the earthquake, the World Food Programme has provided food relief to 115,000 people in Turkey and Syria.	no
世界卫生组织（WHO）则送去了72吨用于外伤处理和紧急手术的医药物资。	The World Health Organization (WHO) sent 72 tons of medical supplies for trauma treatment and emergency surgery.	no

NEWS GOV-MO: 警情通告：司警局呼吁市民提防假冒电讯公司诈骗短讯	NEWS GOV-MO: POLICE Information Notice: THE Provincial Police Department calls on the public to beware of fraudulent SMS messages from fake telecommunications companies	yes
近日司警局接获多宗电信诈骗案，不法分子假冒本澳电讯公司向事主发送附有网站连结的诈骗短信，以积分到期须尽快换领奖赏为饵，诱骗事主登入虚假网站进行兑换。	Recently, the police department of the division received a number of telecommunications fraud cases. Criminals pretended to be local telecommunications companies to send fraudulent text messages with links to websites to the owner, using the points as bait to redeem rewards as soon as possible when they expire, to trick the owner into logging in to the fake website for redemption.	yes
事主按指示输入信用卡资料及验证码，随即收到金融机构通知信用卡出现不明消费记录，怀疑信用卡资料经上述网站被盗取。	The subject entered the credit card information and verification code as instructed, and then received a notification from the financial institution that the credit card had an unknown consumption record, and it was suspected that the credit card information had been stolen through the above-mentioned website.	yes
经查，证实相关电讯公司并无发出上述短讯。	After investigation, it was confirmed that the relevant telecommunications company did not send the above SMS.	yes
司警局呼吁市民，如接获类似手机短讯须提高警惕，切勿登入短讯所载网站连结或提供任何个人资料；若被要求提供信用卡资料、帐户交易密码、交易验证码，更要加倍谨慎，防止信用卡被盗刷。	The Si Police Department urges the public to be vigilant if they receive similar mobile phone SMS messages. Do not log in to the website link contained in the SMS or provide any personal information. If you are asked to provide credit card information, account transaction password, and transaction verification code, you should be more cautious to prevent credit card theft. Swipe.	yes
防骗提示：	Anti-fraud tips：	yes
1. 多关注网络安全资讯，提高个人防范意识；	1. Pay more attention to network security information and raise personal awareness of prevention；	yes
2. 切勿随便登入来历不明的网站并在网站内登记个人及信用卡资料，以防遭人盗用；	2. Do not log in to websites of unknown origin casually and register personal and credit card information on the website to prevent theft.；	yes
3. 警惕假冒网站及钓鱼网站，时刻留意网站网址是否与官方网站完全相符；	3. Be wary of fake websites and phishing websites, and always pay attention to whether the website url exactly matches the official website；	yes
4. 为手机、移动装置或电脑安装防毒软件，并定期更新；	4. Install anti-virus software for mobile phones, mobile devices or computers and update them regularly；	yes
5. 怀疑遇到诈骗或其他犯罪时，应立即致电司警局防诈骗查询热线8800 7777或报案热线993求助。	5. If you suspect that you have encountered fraud or other crimes, you should immediately call the anti-fraud enquiry hotline of the Police Department at 8800 7777 or the crime reporting hotline at 993 for help.	no
NEWS GOV-MO: 香港大型考察团走访澳门旅游景点设施 吸引港客并拓展港澳“联线同游”	NEWS GOV-MO: A large-scale Hong Kong delegation visited Macau's tourist attractions and facilities to attract Hong Kong tourists and expand “online travel” between Hong Kong and Macao	yes
旅游局组织由香港政府旅游部门、旅游业界及传媒代表组成超过100人的大型香港考察团到澳门，两天(10日及11日)的日程除了工作会议和业界洽谈，香港旅行社业界及传媒代表更分批走访澳门多个旅游景点、酒店及旅游相关设施，为香港市场引进最新的澳门旅游产品，同时促进两地文旅联动，共拓港澳“联线同游”市场。	MGTO organized a large-scale Hong Kong delegation of more than 100 people composed of representatives of the tourism department of the Hong Kong Government, the tourism industry and the media to Macao. In addition to work meetings and industry negotiations, the two-day (10th and 11th) schedule, representatives of the Hong Kong travel agency industry and the media also visited a number of tourist attractions, hotels and tourism-related facilities in Macao in batches to introduce the latest Macao tourism products to the Hong Kong market, while promoting cultural tourism linkage between the two places to jointly expand the “online travel” market in Hong Kong and Macao.	yes
亲临考察引入澳门旅游新玩法	Visit in person to introduce a new way of playing Macau tourism	yes
是次香港百人大型考察团包括香港政府旅游相关部门领导主管、60多位来自旅行社及港澳跨境交通营运商的代表以及约30位分别来自旅游杂志及报章的记者、旅游社交媒体、网络媒体代表及博客/网红等，亲临澳门交流考察，了解澳门最新旅游资源，香港业界及媒体将澳门旅游的新玩法带给香港居民以至访港旅客，藉香港交通枢纽的优势，拓展港澳“联线同游”市场。	The large-scale delegation of 100 people in Hong Kong included leaders of tourism-related departments of the Hong Kong Government, more than 60 representatives from travel agencies and cross-border transportation operators between Hong Kong and Macao, and about 30 reporters from travel magazines and newspapers, travel social media, online media representatives and bloggers/net celebrities, etc., to visit Macao for exchanges and visits to learn about Macao's latest tourism resources. The Hong Kong industry and the media will bring the new gameplay of Macao tourism to Hong Kong residents and visitors to Hong Kong, taking advantage of the advantages of Hong Kong's transportation hub to expand the “online travel” market in Hong Kong and Macao.	yes

吸引香港旅客 拓展港澳“联线同游”	Attract Hong Kong tourists to expand “online travel” between Hong Kong and Macao	yes
乘着通关复常的契机，旅游局铺开了香港市场的宣传攻势及推出各项优惠，其中包括推出了往返港澳交通票务优惠，以崭新的宣传片于线上线下平台投放广告等。	Taking advantage of the opportunity for customs clearance to return to normal, MGTO has launched a promotional campaign in the Hong Kong market and launched various discounts, including the launch of transportation ticketing discounts to and from Hong Kong and Macao, and the use of brand-new promotional videos to advertise on online and offline platforms.	yes
继上月邀请香港旅游业界领袖来澳交流考察及香港网红亲身体验澳门“旅游+”，这次再度组织香港旅游业界及传媒代表来澳考察，加大市场推广力度，吸引香港旅客来澳留宿消费，两地业界更洽商携手拓展港澳“联线同游”市场，共拓内地以至海外市场，促进两地旅游业复苏。	Following last month's invitation to leaders of the Hong Kong tourism industry to come to Macao for exchange and investigation and Hong Kong net celebrities to experience Macao's “Tourism+” firsthand, this time, representatives of the Hong Kong tourism industry and the media were once again organized to visit Macao to increase marketing efforts and attract Hong Kong tourists to stay in Macao for consumption. The two industries have also negotiated to work together to expand the “online travel” market in Hong Kong and Macao, jointly expand the Mainland and overseas markets, and promote the recovery of the tourism industry in the two places.	yes
习近平回信勉励援中非中国医疗队队员 以仁心仁术造福当地人民 以实际行动讲好中国故事 - 滚动新闻 - 湖南日报网 - 华声在线	Xi Jinping wrote back and encouraged the members of the Chinese medical team to aid Central Africa to benefit the local people with benevolence and benevolence. 习近平回信勉励援中非中国医疗队队员 以仁心仁术造福当地人民 以实际行动讲好中国故事	Xi Jinping wrote back and encouraged the members of the Chinese medical team to aid Central Africa to benefit the local people with benevolence and benevolence, and to tell a good Chinese story with practical actions.	yes
2023-02-11 13:09:10 [来源:新华社] [责编:李絮枫] 字体:【大 中 小】	2023-02-11 13:09:10 [Source: Xinhua News Agency] [Responsible Editor: Li Xufeng] Font: 【Large, Medium and small】	yes
新华社北京2月10日电 中共中央总书记、国家主席、中央军委主席习近平2月9日给第19批援助中非共和国的中国医疗队队员回信，向他们以及广大援外医疗队员致以问候并提出殷切期望。	Xinhua News Agency, Beijing, February 10th, Xi Jinping, General Secretary of the Central Committee of the Communist Party of China, President of the State, and Chairman of the Central Military Commission, wrote back to the 19th batch of Chinese medical team members assisting the Central African Republic on February 9th, extending greetings to them and the majority of foreign medical team members and putting forward ardent expectations.	yes
习近平在回信中说，你们在中非克服工作生活上的困难，用心服务当地民众，既是救死扶伤的白衣天使，也是传递情谊的友好使者。	In his reply, Xi Jinping said that you have overcome the difficulties of work and life in Central Africa and served the local people with your heart. You are not only angels in white who save lives and injuries, but also friendly messengers who convey friendship.	yes
今年是中国援外医疗队派遣60周年，谨向正在和曾经执行援外医疗任务的同志们致以诚挚的慰问。	This year marks the 60th anniversary of the dispatch of the Chinese foreign aid medical team. I would like to extend my sincere condolences to the comrades who are and have performed foreign aid medical missions.	yes
习近平指出，中国人民热爱和平、珍视生命，援外医疗就是生动的体现。	Xi Jinping pointed out that the Chinese people love peace and cherish life, and foreign aid medical care is a vivid embodiment.	yes
希望你们不忘初心、牢记使命，大力弘扬不畏艰苦、甘于奉献、救死扶伤、大爱无疆的中国医疗队精神，以仁心仁术造福当地人民，以实际行动讲好中国故事，为推动构建人类卫生健康共同体作出更大贡献。	I hope you will not forget your original intention and keep in mind your mission, and vigorously carry forward the spirit of the Chinese medical team that is not afraid of hardships, willing to give, saving lives and injuries, and boundless love, so as to benefit the local people with benevolence and benevolence, tell the Chinese story well with practical actions, and make greater contributions to promoting the construction of a human health community.	yes
援外医疗是我国援外工作的重要内容。	Foreign aid medical care is an important content of our country's foreign aid work.	yes
1963年，我国向阿尔及利亚派出第一支援外医疗队。	In 1963, my country sent the first foreign medical team to Algeria.	yes
60年来，累计向非洲、亚洲、美洲、欧洲和大洋洲的76个国家和地区派遣医疗队员3万人次，诊治患者2.9亿人次，赢得国际社会广泛赞誉。	Over the past 60 years, a total of 30,000 medical personnel have been dispatched to 76 countries and regions in Africa, Asia, the Americas, Europe and Oceania, and 290 million patients have been treated, which has won wide praise from the international community.	no
目前，援外医疗队在全球56个国家的115个医疗点工作，其中近一半在偏远艰苦地区。	At present, foreign aid medical teams work in 115 medical sites in 56 countries around the world, nearly half of which are in remote and difficult areas.	no

（综合11日电）	(Comprehensive 11th)	yes
Google新推出的人工智能聊天机器人Bard出师不利，在宣传短片中“答错问题”，导致Google母公司Alphabet股价周三一度急挫8.9%，跌破100美元大关，市值蒸发1100亿美元（约4765亿令吉），截至周五闭市报94.57美元。	Google's newly launched artificial intelligence chatbot Bard was unfavorable. As of Friday's close, the market was at 94.57 US dollars.	yes

In the video, someone asked Bard: “Can I tell my 9-year-old about the new discoveries of the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST)?"	yes
”Bard在回答中提到该望远镜曾拍摄到太阳系外行星的第一张照片。	"Bard mentioned in his answer that the telescope had taken the first picture of an extrasolar planet.	yes

新加坡旅游业复苏强劲 入境旅客比2021年增长19倍	Singapore's tourism industry has recovered strongly, and inbound tourists have increased 19 times over 2021.	yes
（综合11日电）新加坡旅游局近日公布，预计2023年到访新加坡的国际旅客人次可达1200万至1400万，将带来约180亿至210亿新元的旅游收益；旅客人次和旅游收入将恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约67%至75%的水平；2024年旅游业实现全面复苏的可能性很大。	(Comprehensive 11th) The Singapore Tourism Board recently announced that it is expected that the number of international tourists visiting Singapore in 2023 will reach 12 million to 14 million, which will bring about S新18 billion to S新21 billion in tourism revenue; the number of tourists and tourism revenue will return to the level of about 67% to 75% before the new crown epidemic in 2019; it is very likely that the tourism industry will achieve a full recovery in 2024.	yes
2022年新加坡旅游市场逐步重新启动和恢复。	The Singapore tourism market will gradually restart and resume in 2022.	yes
新加坡旅游局最新发布的统计数据显示，2022年入境旅客从2021年的33.06万人次增长19倍，达到630万人次，超越旅游局早前预估的400万至600万人次，游客已经恢复至疫情前33%的水平。	The latest statistics released by the Singapore Tourism Board show that inbound tourists in 2022 have increased 19 times from 330,600 in 2021 to 6.3 million, surpassing the Tourism Board's earlier estimate of 4 million to 6 million, and tourists have returned to the pre-epidemic level of 33%.	yes
2022年1月至9月，新加坡旅游收入共计89.6亿新元，预计2022年全年旅游收入可达138亿至143亿新元，比2021年的18.9亿新元增长6倍至7倍，已经恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约50%至52%的水平。	From January to September 2022, Singapore's tourism revenue totaled S新8.96 billion. It is expected that the annual tourism revenue in 2022 will reach S新13.8 billion to S新14.3 billion, an increase of 6 to 7 times from S新1.89 billion in 2021, and it has returned to the level of about 50% to 52% before the New Crown epidemic in 2019.	yes

2022年4月，政府宣布拨款近5亿新元用来刺激旅游业复苏。	In April 2022, the Government announced an allocation of nearly S新500 million to stimulate the recovery of the tourism industry.	yes
旅游局日前宣布，将计划在未来两年从这笔预算中拨出1.1亿新元，推出更多商业和休闲活动吸引旅客回流。	The Tourism Bureau recently announced that it plans to allocate S新110 million from this budget in the next two years to launch more commercial and leisure activities to attract tourists back.	yes
为了使健康养生成为新加坡的旅游亮点之一，新加坡旅游局在2022年11月23日发布了一份意向征集活动，计划在新加坡南部海岸开发一个健康养生景点。	In order to make health and health one of Singapore's tourism highlights, the Singapore Tourism Board released a solicitation of intent on November 23, 2022, planning to develop a health and health attraction on the southern coast of Singapore.	yes
新加坡旅游局体育与康养旅游执行署长王凌丽说，近年来，越来越多的游客把身体健康放在各项考虑因素的首位。	Wang Lingli, Executive Director of Sports and Health Tourism of the Singapore Tourism Board, said that in recent years, more and more tourists have put physical health at the top of various considerations.	yes
在拥有滨海湾花园、滨海堤坝的滨海南区开发一个健康养生景点，有望为新加坡的旅游业和经济作出贡献，让游客在新加坡消费并逗留更久。	The development of a health and health attraction in the Southern Marina District, which owns Gardens by the Bay and Marina Embankment, is expected to contribute to Singapore's tourism and economy, allowing tourists to spend and stay in Singapore longer.	no
新加坡旅游局局长陈建隆表示，未来几年内，健康养生将成为新加坡旅游产品的重要组成部分。	Chen Jianlong, director of the Singapore Tourism Board, said that in the next few years, health and health will become an important part of Singapore's tourism products.	no
新冠疫情提升了公众对于身体和心理健康的认知和需求。	The new Crown epidemic has increased public awareness and demand for physical and mental health.	no
为此，过去两年旅游局一直向本地公众和国际游客推广健康养生项目。	To this end, the Tourism Bureau has been promoting health programs to the local public and international tourists in the past two years.	no

The number of employees in the aviation industry has also returned to the level of about 90% before the epidemic.	no

Q：请问重阳投资，如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势？	Q: What does Chongyang Investment think of the US non-farm payrolls data for January that exceeded expectations and future trends?	yes
A：2月3日美国劳工部公布2023年1月非农就业数据，新增非农就业51.7万人，大幅高于市场预期的18.9万人；失业率降至3.4%，为近50年以来的最低位；时薪同比增速4.4%，环比增速0.3%，略有放缓。	A: On February 3, the U.S. Department of Labor released non-farm payrolls data for January 2023, with 517,000 new non-farm payrolls, which was significantly higher than the 189,000 expected by the market; the unemployment rate fell to 3.4%, the lowest level in nearly 50 years; hourly wages grew by 4.4% year-on-year, and the growth rate was 0.3% sequentially, a slight slowdown.	yes
从总量上来看，本次数据存在很多一次性和技术性因素的扰动，比如罢工返岗的教职工、调查统计口径的修正、季调因子的更新，后续可能将有所修正（参考2022年1月新增非农由50.4万人下修至36.4万人），非农就业或不像数据体现的那样强劲。	From the overall point of view, there are many one-time and technical factors in the data this time, such as the number of faculty and staff returning from strikes, the revision of survey statistics, and the update of seasonal adjustment factors. There may be revisions in the future (refer to the new non-farm payrolls in January 2022 from 504,000 to 364,000), non-farm payrolls may not be as strong as the data shows.	yes
从结构上来看，高科技企业裁员影响仍在，但占比较低；高接触性服务业如休闲酒店、教育保健等新增就业大幅回升，数据显示服务业劳动力缺口仍存。	From a structural point of view, the impact of layoffs in high-tech enterprises is still there, but the proportion is relatively low; new employment in high-contact service industries such as leisure hotels, education and health care has rebounded sharply, and data show that the labor gap in the service industry still exists.	yes
结合同样大超预期的服务业PMI、岗位空缺和劳动力缺口数据的回升和消费信贷数据的强势，我们判断经过极端天气和节假日后美国服务业迎来了快速修复。	Combined with the equally larger-than-expected service industry PMI, the rebound in job vacancies and labor gap data, and the strength of consumer credit data, we judge that the U.S. service industry has ushered in a rapid repair after extreme weather and holidays.	yes
我们认为，在不经过衰退的情况下美国就业市场的供需紧张难以改善。	We believe that the tight supply and demand in the U.S. job market will be difficult to improve without a recession.	yes
目前美国劳动力市场尚有500余万的供给缺口，而劳动参与率上行缓慢，尤其是25-54岁劳动参与率已经接近疫情前高点。	At present, there is still a supply gap of more than 5 million in the U.S. labor market, and the labor participation rate is rising slowly, especially the labor participation rate of 25-54 years old is close to the pre-epidemic high.	yes
除此之外，由于美国居民超额储蓄和消费信贷的强势，消费需求的强劲将促使紧缩政策对就业市场的影响进一步滞后。	In addition, due to the excess savings of U.S. residents and the strength of consumer credit, the strength of consumer demand will cause the impact of tightening policies on the job market to lag further.	yes

(hereinafter referred to as “Shanshan Holdings”), the main body of the certification, published an obituary. Invalid treatment.	yes
上世纪80年代，郑永刚担任国营棉纺厂的厂长，随着调任，1989年郑永刚成为杉杉股份的前身宁波云港服装总厂的厂长。	In the 1980s, Zheng Yonggang served as the director of the state-owned cotton spinning factory. With the transfer, Zheng Yonggang became the director of Ningbo Yungang Garment Factory, the predecessor of Shanshan Shares, in 1989.	yes
2022年12月，在第二十届中国企业领袖年会暨第二十二届中国企业未来之星年会上，郑永刚在演讲中称，在上世纪90年代的中国西服市场，杉杉品牌的市占率曾高达37 % 。	In December 2022, at the 20th Annual Meeting of Chinese Business Leaders and the 22nd Annual Meeting of Future Stars of Chinese Companies, Zheng Yonggang said in his speech that in the Chinese suit market in the 1990s, the market share of the Shanshan brand was as high as 37%.	yes
1996年杉杉股份（600884.SH）上市，成为中国服装业第一家上市公司。	In 1996, Shanshan Shares (600884.SH ) Listed, becoming the first listed company in China's garment industry.	yes
就在服装业务如日中天时，杉杉集团却开始转型，因为郑永刚意识到 ， “ 一旦市场放开，中国品牌自然会形成一个梯队式品牌市场，杉杉西服想一直独领风骚，长期成为国人的国服的可能性不大 ” 。	Just when the clothing business was in full swing, Shanshan Group began to transform, because Zheng Yonggang realized that "once the market is liberalized, Chinese brands will naturally form an echelon brand market. Shanshan suits want to dominate for a long time, and it is unlikely that they will become the national service of Chinese people for a long time.”	yes

战略方向确定后，杉杉开始寻找合作，那时候鞍山热能院为鞍钢配套的炭素研究所在做国家863课题，科研经费不够，于是杉杉和鞍山热能院碳素研究所签署合作协议，共同推动国家863课题“中间相炭微球”项目产业化，从事负极材料的研发、生产和销售，在国内实现负极材料的商用推广。	After the strategic direction was determined, Shanshan began to look for cooperation. At that time, the carbon Research Institute of Anshan Institute of Thermal Energy supporting Ansteel was working on the national 863 project, and the scientific research funds were not enough, so Shanshan and the Carbon Research Institute of Anshan Institute of Thermal Energy signed a cooperation agreement to jointly promote the industrialization of the National 863 project “Intermediate phase carbon microspheres” project, engaged in the research and development, production and sales of anode materials, and realize the commercial promotion of anode materials in China.	yes
2001年，杉杉股份实现中间相炭微球的规模化生产，开始国产化替代，取代日本成为国内中间相炭微球主要供应商。	In 2001, Shanshan Co., Ltd. realized the large-scale production of intermediate-phase carbon microspheres and began to replace them with localization, replacing Japan as the main supplier of intermediate-phase carbon microspheres in China.	no

Except for Zheng Yonggang as the chairman, people from Shanshan enterprises are not sent to Shanjin and adopt an authorized operation method. 据Wind数据显示，截至2022年底，国内共有公募基金管理人156家，管理基金规模约26万亿元；公募基金份额登记机构167家，公募基金销售机构411家。	According to Wind data, by the end of 2022, there are 156 public fund managers in China, with a fund size of about 26 trillion yuan under management; 167 public fund share registration agencies and 411 public fund sales agencies.	yes
各份额登记机构账户体系相互独立，缺乏行业统一的查询渠道。	The account systems of each share registration agency are independent of each other, and there is a lack of a unified inquiry channel for the industry.	yes
有行业人士表示，2021年末我国基金投资者超过7.2亿人，也就是说，全国有一半人都投资了基金产品。	Some industry sources said that at the end of 2021, there were more than 720 million fund investors in our country, that is to say, half of the people in the country invested in fund products.	yes
此前，投资者需要通过不同销售机构查询购买情况，而通过“基金E账户”可以查询所有销售渠道购买的情况，持有基金情况一目了然。	Previously, investors needed to check the purchase status through different sales agencies, and through the “Fund E account”, they could check the purchase status of all sales channels, and the status of holding funds was clear at a glance.	yes
“基金E账户”APP是什么？	What is the ”Fund E Account" APP?	no
据相关文件介绍，“基金E账户”APP 是中国结算经中国证监会批准开发建设的公募基金行业门户手机应用，可为投资者提供全市场公募基金产品场外份额持有情况的一站式查询。	According to relevant documents, the “Fund E Account” APP is a public fund industry portal mobile application developed and built by China Clearing with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission. It can provide investors with a one-stop query on the OTC share holdings of public fund products in the whole market.	no
投资者可以通过“基金E账户”方便、快捷地掌握自己通过全市场各销售渠道购买的各基金管理人旗下公募基金产品场外份额的持有情况，全面提升查询效率。	Through the “Fund E account”, investors can easily and quickly grasp the holdings of the OTC shares of the public fund products of each fund manager purchased through various sales channels in the market, and comprehensively improve the efficiency of inquiries.	no
具体来说，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”查询到的信息包括：在全市场各公募基金管理人处开立的基金账户信息、在公募基金销售机构处开立的交易账户信息以及持有的包括公开募集证券投资基金以及证券公司设立管理的投资者人数不受200人限制的集合资产管理计划等产品的场外份额持有情况。	Specifically, the information that investors can query through the “Fund E Account” includes: fund account information opened at various public fund managers in the market, trading account information opened at public fund sales agencies, and OTC share holdings of products including publicly raised securities investment funds and collective asset management plans that are not limited to 200 investors established and managed by securities companies.	no
上海证券基金评价研究中心业务负责人刘亦千向经济观察网记者表示，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”App一站式获知其所有的场外公募基金持有情况，帮助其找回“被遗忘的资产”，更重要的是为客户实现了综合基金投资情况的全账户信息归集，帮助客户更及时、准确、完整的掌握自身投资情况，从而更好地优化自身的基金组合配置，更好地规划自身的财务安排。	Liu Yiqian, head of the business of the Shanghai Securities Fund Evaluation Research Center, told reporters from the Economic Observation Network that investors can learn about all their OTC public fund holdings through the “Fund E Account” App in one stop, helping them retrieve “forgotten assets”, and more importantly, for customers to achieve a comprehensive fund investment situation. The full account information is collected to help customers more timely, accurate and complete grasp of their own investment situation, so as to better optimize their own fund portfolio allocation and better plan their own financial arrangements.	no
如何注册使用？	How to register for use?	no
记者注意到，目前，“基金E账户”APP已在华为、苹果、小米、OPPO、vivo等手机应用商店上架，但APP尚处于公开试运行阶段，注册需要填写邀请码，投资者可以联系所持有基金的基金管理人获取。	The reporter noticed that at present, the “Fund E Account” APP has been listed on mobile app stores such as Huawei, Apple, Xiaomi, OPPO, vivo, etc., but the APP is still in the public trial operation stage. You need to fill in the invitation code to register. Investors can contact the fund manager of the fund they hold to obtain it.	no
上海一家中大型公募基金客服人员向经济观察网记者提供了一个6位数的邀请码，并告诉记者，“APP试运行阶段，中国结算提供给每个基金管理人一定数量的邀请码，投资者电话过来获取，我们都会提供。	The customer service staff of a large and medium-sized public equity fund in Shanghai provided a 6-digit invitation code to a reporter from <url>, and told the reporter, “During the trial operation of the APP, China Clearing provides each fund manager with a certain number of invitation codes. Investors call to get them, and we will provide them.	no
等试运行结束后，开放用户注册时就不用邀请码了。	After the trial operation is over, the invitation code will not be used when the user registration is opened.	no
”	”	no
记者根据证监会官网公示的“基金E账户”下载及使用说明相关文件进行了账户注册并完成查询，整个过程耗时仅几分钟，主要分为四步：用户注册、实名认证、基金账户绑定、公募基金查询。	The reporter registered the account and completed the inquiry according to the relevant documents of the “Fund E Account” download and usage instructions published on the official website of the Securities and Exchange Commission. The whole process took only a few minutes and was mainly divided into four steps: user registration, real-name authentication, fund account binding, and public fund inquiry.	no
通过实名认证这一步之后，点击“资产”基金绑定按钮，记者通过各个基金销售平台购买的所有基金产品都呈现在绑定选项列表中（可绑定账户），完成绑定后就可以直观看到所投基金总资产并可以开始使用查询功能了。	After passing the real-name authentication step, click the ”Assets" fund binding button. All fund products purchased by reporters through each fund sales platform are presented in the list of binding options (accounts can be bound). After the binding is completed, you can visually see the total assets of the invested fund and you can start using the query function.	no
值得注意的是，“基金E账户”仅为投资者提供查询服务，并不能进行申赎买卖。	It is worth noting that the "Fund E Account" only provides investors with inquiry services and cannot be used for redemption transactions.	no
“基金 E 账户”所显示的数据日期一般为用户进行查询的日期（T日)往前推三个交易日。	The data date displayed in the “Fund E Account” is generally the date on which the user made the query (T day), which is pushed forward by three trading days.	no
比如，在2 月10日打开“基金E账户”，资产页所显示的总资产、基金份额、基金净值对应日期为该日期往前推三个交易日，即2月7日。	For example, if the “Fund E Account” is opened on February 10, the corresponding date of total assets, fund shares, and fund equity displayed on the asset page is three trading days before that date, that is, February 7.	no

中国鼓励拉高生育率 到高校催捐精 质量高标准	China encourages raising the fertility rate to colleges and universities to urge high quality standards for sperm donation	yes

阿拉斯加上空被击落的 “物体”究竟是什么？	What exactly was the “object" that was shot down over Alaska?	yes
扑朔迷离，猜测纷纷	Bewildered, speculations have followed	yes
美国军方周五（2月10日）下午再次动用美国最先进的隐身喷气战机F-22击落了一个在美国阿拉斯加上空飞行的尚未确定身份的物体。	The U.S. military once again used the F-22, the most advanced stealth jet fighter in the United States, to shoot down an unidentified object flying over Alaska in the afternoon of Friday (February 10).	yes
击落的地点距离阿拉斯加海岸十英里。	The location of the shooting down was ten miles from the coast of Alaska.	yes
这是美军在不到一周的时间里第二次击落空中飞行物体。	This is the second time the US military has shot down a flying object in the air in less than a week.	yes
上周六，来自中国的一个间谍气球在美国领空上漂移数日后在美国南卡罗莱纳州沿岸附近上空被击毁。	On Saturday, a spy balloon from China was destroyed in the sky near the coast of South Carolina after drifting in U.S. airspace for several days.	yes
五角大楼说，第二个被击落的物体于周四晚上首次进入美国领空，在阿拉斯加东北部上空移动时被美国军方跟踪，飞行高度为1.2万米（4万英尺），其大小与一辆小型汽车差不多，与先前被击落的那个中国间谍气球相比要小很多。	The Pentagon said the second downed object entered U.S. airspace for the first time on Thursday night and was tracked by the U.S. military as it moved over northeast Alaska. It flew at an altitude of 12,000 meters (40,000 feet) and was about the size of a small car. It is much smaller than the Chinese spy balloon that was shot down earlier.	yes
五角大楼还认为，目前没有迹象显示，这个物体是可操纵的。	The Pentagon also believes that there is currently no indication that this object is maneuverable.	yes
白宫国家安全委员会战略沟通协调员约翰·科比周五表示，虽然这个在高空飞行的物体的具体样子尚不清楚，但它“对民航飞机的安全构成了合理的威胁”。	John Kirby, the strategic communication coordinator of the White House National Security Council, said on Friday that although the specific appearance of the object flying at high altitude is not yet clear, it “poses a reasonable threat to the safety of civil aviation aircraft.”	yes
科比表示，这个物体与美国境内发现的那个间谍气球不同，它上面没有悬挂“有效载荷”。	Kobe said that this object is different from the spy balloon found in the United States, and there is no “payload” hanging on it.	yes
科比说，“我们把它称为一个‘物体’是我们目前能够作出的最好的描述”。	Kobe said, “We call it an ‘object’ is the best description we can currently make.”	no
拜登总统在下令击落这个物体之前听取了五角大楼的建议，他作出这个决定的时候“非常谨慎”，科比补充说。	President Biden listened to the advice of the Pentagon before ordering the shooting down of the object. He made this decision “very cautiously,” Kobe added.	no

但这些信息还无法回答基本问题，比如这个物体究竟是什么东西，它属于哪个国家，它在执行什么任务。	But this information still cannot answer basic questions, such as what exactly is this object, which country it belongs to, and what tasks it is performing.	no
目前网上许多的分析和猜测认为，这可能又是一只中国气球。	At present, many analyses and speculations on the Internet believe that this may be another Chinese balloon.	no
它可能与入侵美国领空的那只间谍气球和在拉美上空飘动的那只中国气球一样都来自中国，它们在不同地点执行某种任务。	It may be the same as the spy balloon that invaded U.S. airspace and the Chinese balloon that fluttered over Latin America. They came from China and performed certain missions in different locations.	no
